*   [Session Placeholder](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-backtesting/backtesters/strategy-scripting/placeholders#session-placeholder)
    
*   [Strategy Statistics Placeholders](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-backtesting/backtesters/strategy-scripting/placeholders#strategy-statistics-placeholders)
    
*   [External Placeholders](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-backtesting/backtesters/strategy-scripting/placeholders#external-placeholders)
    
*   [User Defined Placeholders (UDP)](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-backtesting/backtesters/strategy-scripting/placeholders#user-defined-placeholders-udp)
    
*   [Backtester Trigger Placeholders](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-backtesting/backtesters/strategy-scripting/placeholders#backtester-trigger-placeholders)
    
*   [Backtester (S&O) Trigger Placeholders](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-backtesting/backtesters/strategy-scripting/placeholders#backtester-s%26o-trigger-placeholders)
    
*   [Backtester (PAC) Trigger Placeholders](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-backtesting/backtesters/strategy-scripting/placeholders#backtester-pac-trigger-placeholders)
    
*   [Backtester (OSC) Trigger Placeholders](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-backtesting/backtesters/strategy-scripting/placeholders#backtester-osc-trigger-placeholders)
    

Placeholders are strings that refer to a specific series of values or events, and have the form `{placeholder_title}`, where `placeholder_title` is the name of the placeholder to access and `{}` makes sure the string is recognized as a placeholder. With scripted strategies, placeholders allow accessing market data such as ohlc prices, volume, but also strategy data such as net profit, winrate, entry prices…etc.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-backtesting/backtesters/strategy-scripting/placeholders#market-data-placeholders)

Market Data Placeholders
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Market data placeholder allows referencing typical market data such as ohlc prices and volume. These placeholders are available for all toolkits.

| Placeholder | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `{open}` | Open price of the bar |
| `{high}` | High price of the bar |
| `{low}` | Low price of the bar |
| `{close}` | Close price of the bar |
| `{hl2}` | Median price `(high + low) / 2` |
| `{ohlc4}` | Average price `(open + high + low + close) / 4` |
| `{hlc3}` | Typical price `(high + low + close) / 3` |
| `{hlcc4}` | Weighted average of hlc prices `(high + low + 2 * close) / 4` |
| `{volume}` | Volume for the bar |
| `{range}` | Difference between High and Low prices |
| `{tr}` | True Range |

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-backtesting/backtesters/strategy-scripting/placeholders#time-related-placeholders)

Time Related Placeholders
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Time placeholder allows referencing time related information such as the bar hour and minute, day, bar index…etc. These placeholders are available for all toolkits.

| Placeholder | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `{barindex}` | Index of the current bar |
| `{last_barindex}` | Index of the most recent bar |
| `{second}` | Current bar second |
| `{minute}` | Current bar minute |
| `{hour}` | Current bar hour |
| `{dayofweek}` | Current bar day of the week ranging from 1 to 7, with 1 for sunday |
| `{dayofmonth}` | Current bar day of the month |
| `{weekofyear}` | Current bar week of the year |
| `{month}` | Current bar month of the year |
| `{year}` | Current bar year (with timezone) |
| `{time}` | Unix timestamp of the bar |
| `{unix_ts}` | Unix timestamp of the bar (Deprecated, use `{time}`) |
| `{timeframe}` | Chart timeframe in minutes |
| `{hhmm-hhmm}` | Session placeholder, `True` when the bar is located within the specific session interval, see [here](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-backtesting/backtesters/strategy-scripting/placeholders#session-placeholder)<br> for more information |
| `{YYYY-MM-DDThh:mm:ss±hh:mm}` | Datestring placeholder, equal to the timestamp of the specified date, see [here](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-backtesting/backtesters/strategy-scripting/placeholders#datestring-placeholder)<br> for more information |

Note that `{dayofweek}` returns the day based on the time of the bar’s open. For overnight sessions (e.g. EURUSD, where Monday session starts on Sunday, 17:00) this value can be lower by 1 than the day of the trading day.

The timezone for the time related placeholders (with the exception of `time`, and the datestring placeholder) is defined by the `Timezone` dropdown setting, defining the timezone using UTC. Default value is `exchange`, which uses the exchange timezones to get the value of the time related placeholders.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-backtesting/backtesters/strategy-scripting/placeholders#datestring-placeholder)

Datestring Placeholder

You can easily define dates and optionally th time and timezone using the **Datestring** placeholder, following the ISO 8601 standard. The syntax of the placeholder is as follows:

Example

    {YYYY-MM-DDThh:mm:ss±hh:mm}
    

*   `YYYY`: Year
*   `MM`: Month
*   `DD`: Day
*   `hh`: Hour
*   `mm`: Minute
*   `±hh:mm`: Timezone offset, default timezone is UTC-0 (optional)

The **Datestring** placeholder is not affected by the **Timezone** setting

This placeholder can be useful alongside `{time}` to constraint the evaluation of conditions to a specific date interval. For example:

Example

    {close} > {open} and {time} >= {2025-01-01}
    

The above script will only trigger if the closing price is above the opening price while the time is on or after January 1st, 2025. Dates and times are separated by `T`, for example `{2025-01-01T04:00}`. `±hh:mm` can be used to offset the timezones, as such if the timezone of interest is the New York timezone (UTC-4), we would use:

Example

    {2025-01-01T04:00-04:00}
    

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-backtesting/backtesters/strategy-scripting/placeholders#session-placeholder)

Session Placeholder

You can easily detect if the current bar is within a specific session (time interval) by using the session placeholder with pattern `{hhmm-hhmm}`, where `hh` is the hour and `mm` the minute. The value of this placeholder will be `True` when the bar time is located between the start time `{hhmm-` and end time `-hhmm}`. For example, if we want to detect when the bar is located in the session starting at 14:30 and ending at 16:45 we would simply use:

Example

    {1430-1645}
    

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-backtesting/backtesters/strategy-scripting/placeholders#strategy-statistics-placeholders)

Strategy Statistics Placeholders
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

It is possible to use the actual strategy results made over time as part of our entry or exit conditions using the following data placeholders:

| Placeholder | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `{entry_price}` | Average entry price of the current position |
| `{net_profit}` | Total net profit from all closed trades |
| `{equity}` | Current equity including open trades |
| `{open_profit}` | Unrealized profit/loss of open trades |
| `{gross_profit}` | Total gross profit from winning trades |
| `{gross_loss}` | Total gross loss from losing trades |
| `{gross_profit_percent}` | Gross profit expressed as a percentage |
| `{gross_loss_percent}` | Gross loss expressed as a percentage |
| `{profit_factor}` | Ratio of gross profit to gross loss |
| `{winrate}` | Percentage of closed trades that were wins |
| `{closed_trades}` | Number of closed trades |
| `{open_trades}` | Number of currently open trades |
| `{win_trades}` | Number of winning closed trades |
| `{loss_trades}` | Number of losing closed trades |
| `{avg_trade}` | Average profit/loss per trade |
| `{avg_winning_trade}` | Average profit of winning trades |
| `{avg_losing_trade}` | Average loss of losing trades |
| `{max_drawdown}` | Maximum drawdown in account value |
| `{max_drawdown_percent}` | Max drawdown expressed as a percentage |
| `{max_runup}` | Maximum runup in account value |
| `{max_runup_percent}` | Max runup expressed as a percentage |
| `{position_size}` | Current position size |

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-backtesting/backtesters/strategy-scripting/placeholders#external-placeholders)

External Placeholders
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/0Jdje6xa5PGD9ypH/public/images/alert-scripting/placeholders/external.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=0Jdje6xa5PGD9ypH&q=85&s=02ef9a9a385d0a0a83c06fe39a904140) Users can refer to a series of values outside the toolkit by using external placeholder. A maximum of 3 external placeholders can be used:

*   `{external1}`
*   `{external2}`
*   `{external3}`

In order to use external placeholders, users must first select the external source from the provided dropdowns located in the Strategy Scripting settings. Once selected, external sources can be referred from their respective placeholders.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-backtesting/backtesters/strategy-scripting/placeholders#user-defined-placeholders-udp)

User Defined Placeholders (UDP)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

User defined placeholders (UDPs) are custom placeholders defined by users and assigned to a specific condition set by the user. These placeholders can later be referenced as part of other conditions or UDPs. To define an UDP a line must start with a placeholder with a unique name, followed by an equal sign `=`, then followed by the condition we want to assign to this placeholder, for example `{my_placeholder} = {close} > {open}` Let’s take a more complex example and say we want to go long on a new bullish fair value gap while we also had one on the previous bar. Doing this could involve a long and messy script, to make things easier we can create an UDP that refers to the condition of a bullish fair value gaps:

    {bull_fvg} = {low} > {high[2]} and {close[1]} > {high[2]}
    @long() = {bull_fvg} and {bull_fvg[1]}
    

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-backtesting/backtesters/strategy-scripting/placeholders#backtester-trigger-placeholders)

Get Started

How To Setup LuxAlgo

Once you’ve signed up to any plan on [our website](https://luxalgo.com/pricing)
 — you will be able to see a place to “Connect Accounts” and enter your TradingView username to get instant access to use our exclusive tools compatible with TradingView. In order to use our exclusive tools, you need to open a chart on TradingView. ![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/CDau_eRmDqLaKwqU/public/images/setup-tradingview/image603.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=CDau_eRmDqLaKwqU&q=85&s=88bdb444aa939cc91d196a076459a565) Once your chart is open, click on **Indicators** (or type **/** ) to open the indicator menu, then click on “**Invite-only Scripts**”. You should see the names of each Toolkit, Screener, or Backtester appear in this folder and you can click on one them to add to your chart. Remember, you don’t need to use all of these tools at once. It is suggested for users to explore through our tools to find a couple features that fit most optimally in your trading. ![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/CDau_eRmDqLaKwqU/public/images/setup-tradingview/image571.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=CDau_eRmDqLaKwqU&q=85&s=11e146652b7d3bde0bb50f60a0567ae7)

If you don’t see the invite-only scripts folder or the locks appear red, please first try refreshing your browser/app. If this still doesn’t have them show up, please email [\[email protected\]](https://docs.luxalgo.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#3b484e4b4b54494f7b574e435a575c5415585456)
 with your TradingView username or contact live-chat on our website and our team will grant you access right away.

If you want to quickly access our tools you can add them to your favorites by clicking on the star at the right of their names in the folder. You will then be able to load the starred indicators directly from your favorites tab while on your charts. ![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/CDau_eRmDqLaKwqU/public/images/setup-tradingview/image560.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=CDau_eRmDqLaKwqU&q=85&s=6f4b4a2164411fcc0ab34ae7fa100e5a)

# Sorting Functionality | Oscillator Matrix Screener | LuxAlgo

[Skip to main content](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/screeners/osc/sorting#content-area)

[LuxAlgo home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=9a82ae47268cbdb594f7f904c8dc654f)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=9db2e704694ba3dd9d249afa92f16cc5)](https://docs.luxalgo.com/)

Search...

Navigation

Screener (OSC)

Sorting

![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/CDau_eRmDqLaKwqU/public/images/screeners/sort.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=CDau_eRmDqLaKwqU&q=85&s=86177b3816265d7a3b2beeee79752468) Users can sort certain elements returning/or with an associated numerical information in either a descending or ascending order. This can be useful to see specific tickers first or last depending on the sorted data on the screener. Supported elements for sorting include:

*   Rating
*   Money Flow
*   HyperWave
*   None

When “None” is selected the screener tickers appear as per their order in the Tickers settings.

![Tickers sorted by rating in a descending order](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-_VCBHd2xJR0PihX/public/images/screeners/osc/sorting/sorted.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=-_VCBHd2xJR0PihX&q=85&s=dda7bbe9e63036141d0c0eb57c7f3afa)

# How To Update | Exclusive Tools on TradingView | LuxAlgo

[Skip to main content](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/getting-started/how-to-update#content-area)

[LuxAlgo home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=9a82ae47268cbdb594f7f904c8dc654f)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=9db2e704694ba3dd9d249afa92f16cc5)](https://docs.luxalgo.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Get Started

How To Get Updates

On this page

*   [Applying An Update](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/getting-started/how-to-update#applying-an-update)
    
*   [Receiving Updates Notifications](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/getting-started/how-to-update#receiving-updates-notifications)
    

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/getting-started/how-to-update#applying-an-update)

Applying An Update
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

On Tradingview updates are easy to apply. Once an update is available, refresh your chart, then a purple 🔄 icon will be visible near the indicator title, click on it and click on “Update to latest version”. ![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/how-to-update/update.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=361af347ce61198eb09284afb3ff3c17) You can also apply an update by following these steps:

1.  Refresh your browser or mobile app
2.  Remove the indicator from your chart
3.  Re-add it from your invite-only indicators

The latest version of the indicator should appear.

Make sure to save your **Chart Layout** on Tradingview after successfully installing an update so you can ensure it will stay

![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/how-to-update/image172.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=de98ab6de41a51b66ed482cdb7d5656e)

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/getting-started/how-to-update#receiving-updates-notifications)

Receiving Updates Notifications
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We always announce our updates on our community Discord server & [X Account](https://x.com/LuxAlgo)
. You can also receive update notifications on your TradingView charts directly by going to: `settings -> notifications -> SCRIPTS YOU'VE ADDED TO FAVORITES OR LIKED` ![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/how-to-update/image125.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=4c9e08d21b0fe42c5d68f6acf9d9ef03)

Make sure to follow the LuxAlgo account on [TradingView](https://www.tradingview.com/u/LuxAlgo/#published-scripts)
 to ensure you are notified when we push updates with new features to our exclusive tools!

# Quant Prompting Tips | LuxAlgo

[Skip to main content](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/quant/prompting-tips#content-area)

[LuxAlgo home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=9a82ae47268cbdb594f7f904c8dc654f)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=9db2e704694ba3dd9d249afa92f16cc5)](https://docs.luxalgo.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

✨ Quant

Prompting Tips

On this page

*   [Start Simple](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/quant/prompting-tips#start-simple)
    
*   [Be Specific About the “Result”](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/quant/prompting-tips#be-specific-about-the-%E2%80%9Cresult%E2%80%9D)
    
*   [Break Big Work Into Small Steps](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/quant/prompting-tips#break-big-work-into-small-steps)
    
*   [Ask the Agent to Plan When It’s Complex](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/quant/prompting-tips#ask-the-agent-to-plan-when-it%E2%80%99s-complex)
    
*   [Iterate with Targeted Follow-ups](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/quant/prompting-tips#iterate-with-targeted-follow-ups)
    

Effective prompting is key to getting the best results from Quant. Follow these tips to generate high-quality Pine Script® code efficiently.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/quant/prompting-tips#start-simple)

Start Simple
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Say what you want to build in plain language. **Examples:**

*   “A RSI oscillator with signals.”
*   “An order block detector with breakout signals.”

This gets you moving fast and gives the agent something concrete to scaffold.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/quant/prompting-tips#be-specific-about-the-%E2%80%9Cresult%E2%80%9D)

Be Specific About the “Result”
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Tell Quant what “done” looks like:

*   Expected indicator behavior under specific scenarios
*   How the indicator should look like, with explicit mention of plot/label/line styles, colors, linewidth…etc
*   Tell Quant if the indicator should appear on the chart, or in its own pane

You can use images to provide a more direct answer about what the output should look like.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/quant/prompting-tips#break-big-work-into-small-steps)

Break Big Work Into Small Steps
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Asking Quant to build a complex indicator/strategy/toolkit in a single shot will generally lead to poor results. Instead of “build the whole toolkit,” do:

*   “Start with element A.”
*   “Add element B”
*   “Add element C”
*   “Add alerts”

Incremental prompts reduce bugs, and provide checkpoints you can comeback to.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/quant/prompting-tips#ask-the-agent-to-plan-when-it%E2%80%99s-complex)

Ask the Agent to Plan When It’s Complex
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you’re not sure about the indicator architecture:

> “Break this indicator into steps and propose a plan to achieve it”

Then implement step-by-step.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/quant/prompting-tips#iterate-with-targeted-follow-ups)

Iterate with Targeted Follow-ups
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After the first output, request one change per message:

*   “Add moving average to x.”
*   “Add alert on condition x.”
*   “Add tooltip to these inputs…”

This keeps iterations clean and predictable.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Features](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/quant/features)
[Introduction](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-backtesting/introduction)

# AI Strategy Alerts | Notifications | LuxAlgo

[Skip to main content](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-strategy-alerts/notifications#content-area)

[LuxAlgo home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=9a82ae47268cbdb594f7f904c8dc654f)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=9db2e704694ba3dd9d249afa92f16cc5)](https://docs.luxalgo.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

AI Strategy Alerts

Notifications

On this page

*   [Events](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-strategy-alerts/notifications#events)
    
*   [Alert message](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-strategy-alerts/notifications#alert-message)
    
*   [Placeholders](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-strategy-alerts/notifications#placeholders)
    
*   [In-App Notifications](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-strategy-alerts/notifications#in-app-notifications)
    
*   [Emails](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-strategy-alerts/notifications#emails)
    

![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/043iZqUq2bKrDELT/public/images/ai-strategy-alerts/notifications-menu.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=043iZqUq2bKrDELT&q=85&s=bf67849d9c7b6fd1487ae01b1243d48b) Users can be notified of triggered alerts via in-app notifications and/or emails. The default view when creating or editing an alert displays the notification settings by default and can be accessed at any time by clicking on “Notifications” in the alert menu sidebar.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-strategy-alerts/notifications#events)

Events
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The event toggles determine which strategy events (long, short, exit long, exit short) trigger an in-app or email notification (if enabled).

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-strategy-alerts/notifications#alert-message)

Alert message
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The alert message field determines the content that appears in the in-app notification or email.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-strategy-alerts/notifications#placeholders)

Placeholders

Users might want to include dynamic data in their alert message, such as which strategy event triggered the alert or the strategy’s entry price. This is possible using placeholders. The syntax is `[[placeholder_name]]`. The following placeholders are available.

| Placeholder | Description |     |
| --- | --- | --- |
| \[\[currency\]\] | Currency of the asset the strategy is based on |     |
| \[\[current\_contract\_myy\]\] | For strategies set on futures, current contract traded by the strategy in the format `[ROOT][MONTH_CODE][2 digit YEAR]`, for example `ESZ25` | `string` |
| \[\[current\_contract\_myyyy\]\] | For strategies set on futures, current contract traded by the strategy in the format `[ROOT][MONTH_CODE][4 digit YEAR]`, for example `ESZ2025` | `string` |
| \[\[exchange\]\] | Exchange where the asset is traded |     |
| \[\[strategy\_event\]\] | Event originating from the strategy, options include “long”, “short”, “exit long”, “exit short” |     |
| \[\[strategy\_id\]\] | A unique identifier associated to the strategy |     |
| \[\[strategy\_market\_position\]\] | Current position of the strategy, options include “long”, “short”, “flat” |     |
| \[\[strategy\_name\]\] | Name of the strategy |     |
| \[\[strategy\_order\_action\]\] | Action taken by the strategy, options include “buy” and “sell”. For this placeholder an exit long would lead to the value being “sell” while an exit short would lead to “buy” |     |
| \[\[strategy\_order\_price\]\] | Price at which the order was executed |     |
| \[\[ticker\]\] | Ticker symbol the strategy is based on |     |
| \[\[time\]\] | ISO 8601 datetime (including milliseconds) of the opening time of the candle for which the strategy event occurred. Example `2025-11-17T23:14:52.123Z` | `datetime` |
| \[\[timeframe\]\] | Timeframe the strategy is based on | `number` |
| \[\[timenow\]\] | ISO 8601 datetime (including milliseconds) of the alert being triggered. Example `2025-11-17T23:14:52.123Z` | `datetime` |

Example of a strategy alert message using placeholders:

    Strategy "[[strategy_name]]" triggered a new [[strategy_event]] signal on [[ticker]] ([[timeframe]]m) at price [[strategy_order_price]].
    

Placeholders may be inserted in the message directly through the “Placeholders” dropdown; click a placeholder to insert it.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-strategy-alerts/notifications#in-app-notifications)

In-App Notifications
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/043iZqUq2bKrDELT/public/images/ai-strategy-alerts/toasts.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=043iZqUq2bKrDELT&q=85&s=4c6d05c3910a244cdf3faf0d618c9b4d) In-app notifications display small cards indicating an alert has been triggered. On desktop, they appear at the bottom-right of the screen; on mobile, at the bottom. ![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/043iZqUq2bKrDELT/public/images/ai-strategy-alerts/toasts-expand.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=043iZqUq2bKrDELT&q=85&s=3a5b6bb681dcee303995b9d0cf0a01ea) Hovering over a card shows messages from older alerts. Removing a card displays the next oldest alert (if any) at the top of the list.

Users can edit alerts directly from the cards by clicking the gear icon in the bottom-right.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-strategy-alerts/notifications#emails)

Emails
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/043iZqUq2bKrDELT/public/images/ai-strategy-alerts/email.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=043iZqUq2bKrDELT&q=85&s=dc9efc85c7e91f7c9187ed7af433436f) When a strategy alert is triggered, the user can receive an email at the address associated with their account. To receive emails, enable “Send email” in the Notifications settings at the bottom-right.

Was this page helpful?

# Filtering | Oscillator Matrix Screener | LuxAlgo

[Skip to main content](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/screeners/osc/filtering#content-area)

[LuxAlgo home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=9a82ae47268cbdb594f7f904c8dc654f)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=9db2e704694ba3dd9d249afa92f16cc5)](https://docs.luxalgo.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Screener (OSC)

Filtering

![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-_VCBHd2xJR0PihX/public/images/screeners/osc/filtering/filter.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=-_VCBHd2xJR0PihX&q=85&s=86110a4aff335f246d7e823b36978395)

From the “Screener Elements” settings users are able to filter out undesired information returned by the screener. This is done from the dropdown setting located on each “Screener Elements” settings. Certain elements returning specific information from a list of supported options will have a filter allowing to select a precise option, while elements returning a value on the screener will make use of conditional operators (Above/Below). Users can set a filtering condition on multiple elements, allowing them to display the tickers that respect the user set filtering conditions.

# Quant Features | LuxAlgo

[Skip to main content](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/quant/features#content-area)

[LuxAlgo home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=9a82ae47268cbdb594f7f904c8dc654f)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=9db2e704694ba3dd9d249afa92f16cc5)](https://docs.luxalgo.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

✨ Quant

Features

On this page

*   [Code Generation](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/quant/features#code-generation)
    
*   [Image to Code](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/quant/features#image-to-code)
    
*   [Bug Fixing](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/quant/features#bug-fixing)
    
*   [Pine Script Help](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/quant/features#pine-script-help)
    
*   [Assisted Coding](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/quant/features#assisted-coding)
    

Quant provides a comprehensive set of features designed to help you create, refine, and deploy Pine Script® indicators and strategies. This page covers the core capabilities available in the Quant interface.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/quant/features#code-generation)

Code Generation
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Quant can generate complete Pine Script® code based on your natural language descriptions. When Quant generates code, it appears in a split editor view, allowing you to review the generated script alongside the chat interface. You can copy the generated code using the copy button and paste it directly into TradingView® to add the indicator to your charts. ![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/1FVf4T81OekCpjDK/public/images/quant/code-generation-editor.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=1FVf4T81OekCpjDK&q=85&s=97f1d4f7d0bb1e60c27c235c82efa799)

The code cannot be copied while Quant is actively generating code. Wait for the generation to complete before using the copy button.

Quant leverages its access to both TradingView scripts and LuxAlgo’s proprietary script library to reliably handle niche and complex concepts. This dual knowledge base enables Quant to generate more relevant and code of higher quality.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/quant/features#image-to-code)

Image to Code
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can upload images of indicators or chart setups, by pasting them directly in the prompt input, uploading them from the upload image button, or by clicking on “Generate From Image”, and Quant will analyze the visual representation to generate Pine Script® code that reproduces the indicator’s behavior as closely as possible. ![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/1FVf4T81OekCpjDK/public/images/quant/image-to-code-interface.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=1FVf4T81OekCpjDK&q=85&s=f7f360f5fce18a77776582f59310f53c) Additionally, you can send images during your conversation to provide more context or refine Quant’s understanding of your requirements. This helps Quant better interpret complex visual patterns and generate more accurate code.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/quant/features#bug-fixing)

Bug Fixing
--------------------------------------------------------------------------

Quant can automatically identify and fix errors and warnings in your Pine Script® code. To fix all errors and warnings present in your script, use the “Fix with Quant” button in the editor. ![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/1FVf4T81OekCpjDK/public/images/quant/bug-fixing-interface.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=1FVf4T81OekCpjDK&q=85&s=1e6010199f836d709c6199c38f20bfbc)

Errors prevent the script from running, while warnings won’t prevent execution but may cause unexpected results.

The editor also includes error and warnings highlighting for users more used to this.

You can hover on the error or warning button to get more information about them.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/quant/features#pine-script-help)

Pine Script Help
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Quant has access to the complete Pine Script® knowledge base and can assist you with questions about Pine Script® syntax, functions, best practices, and implementation patterns. Whether you’re learning Pine Script® or need clarification on specific concepts, Quant can provide accurate, context-aware answers based on official Pine Script® documentation.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/quant/features#assisted-coding)

Assisted Coding
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For more experienced Pine Script® developers, Quant can assist with repetitive tasks and complex implementations. The integrated code editor is fully interactive and supports syntax/error highlighting as well as syntax completion, providing a professional coding environment.

The editor cannot be used while Quant is generating code. Wait for code generation to complete before making manual edits.

You can work collaboratively with Quant by making manual edits to the code, and Quant will learn from your changes to assist with subsequent iterations and refinements.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[Introduction](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/quant/introduction)
[Prompting Tips](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/quant/prompting-tips)

⌘I

Assistant

✨ Quant

Introduction

On this page

*   [Documentation](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/quant/introduction#documentation)
    
*   [FAQ](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/quant/introduction#faq)
    
*   [Disclaimer](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/quant/introduction#disclaimer)
    

![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/1FVf4T81OekCpjDK/public/images/quant/introduction-hero.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=1FVf4T81OekCpjDK&q=85&s=16f6157d87767e92106fe59dd256d747) Quant is an AI coding agent specialized in generating and validating Pine Script® indicators and strategies for TradingView®. This documentation will help you understand Quant’s capabilities, learn how to effectively prompt it, and troubleshoot common issues. Quant leverages deep knowledge of Pine Script®, trading indicators, strategies, styling, and validation, built from our extensive library of tools and frameworks developed over 5+ years. This specialization makes Quant superior to generic AI chatbots for trading tool generation.

All users can access Quant [here](https://www.luxalgo.com/quant)
. Users with Premium and Ultimate plans benefit from higher usage limits.

![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/HcpgWZm1QMZwVxg6/public/images/quant/benchmark-chart.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=HcpgWZm1QMZwVxg6&q=85&s=d19a198c9b8018a7c3528b7dab285156)

> _All 100 indicators varied in complexity. An implementation is considered failed if it contains errors (syntax or runtime), return NaN or constant unexpected values, or if the AI did not comply with the user request due to infeasability. Benchmark done on 02/21/2026._

The chart above represents the percentage of correct implementations out of 100 total indicators amongst multiple chatbots.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/quant/introduction#documentation)

Documentation
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Features
--------

Prompting Tips
--------------

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/quant/introduction#faq)

FAQ
----------------------------------------------------------------

How do I get access to Quant?

All users can access Quant [here](https://www.luxalgo.com/quant)
. Users with Premium and Ultimate plans can benefit from higher usage limits.

What are credits?

Credits is the currency system used to control the usage amount a user has with our AI products. The credit balance of an user is shared across both AI Backtesting platform and Quant, our pinescript coding agent.User credits reset every first of the month.

How does Quant differ from ChatGPT or generic AI?

Quant is fully specialized toward trading-tool generation, making it superior to existing AI chatbots that always generate bug-filled, generic indicators & strategies.We built Quant to work with a wizard-level knowledge of Pine Script®, trading indicators, strategies, styling, and validation which was only possible from our own extensive library of tools + frameworks we’ve publicly released & privately hosted over 5+ years.

Can I convert an image of a chart into an indicator?

Yes, you can upload chart screenshots to have Quant reverse-engineer any indicator or marked up strategy into a working replica, often first try. Users can also keep iterating on it in the same chat to generate more features on top as they wish, instantly.

Can Quant generate complete TradingView indicators?

Yes. Quant can generate complete functional TradingView indicators from simple concepts to entire toolkits, which are validated and refined so they are ready to use on your charts.

Do I need to know how to code in Pine Script®?

No. You don’t need to know Pine Script® to use Quant. Quant handles all the coding for you based on your requests.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/quant/introduction#disclaimer)

Disclaimer
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

TradingView® and Pine Script® are registered trademarks of TradingView, Inc. LuxAlgo is not affiliated with TradingView. Please read our [full disclaimer](https://www.luxalgo.com/legal/disclaimer/)
.

Screener (PAC)

Filtering

![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-_VCBHd2xJR0PihX/public/images/screeners/pac/filtering/filter.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=-_VCBHd2xJR0PihX&q=85&s=b5f860f2f6bf5829b258178966eaf82d)

From the “Screener Elements” settings users are able to filter out undesired information returned by the screener. This is done from the dropdown setting located on each “Screener Elements” settings. Certain elements returning specific information from a list of supported options will have a filter allowing to select a precise option, while elements returning a value on the screener will make use of conditional operators (Above/Below). Users can set a filtering condition on multiple elements, allowing them to display the tickers that respect the user set filtering conditions.

# Elements | Price Action Concepts Screener | LuxAlgo

[Skip to main content](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/screeners/pac/elements#content-area)

[LuxAlgo home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=9a82ae47268cbdb594f7f904c8dc654f)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=9db2e704694ba3dd9d249afa92f16cc5)](https://docs.luxalgo.com/)

Search...

Navigation

Screener (PAC)

Elements

On this page

*   [Screener Elements](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/screeners/pac/elements#screener-elements)
    
*   [Ratings](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/screeners/pac/elements#ratings)
    
*   [Indicator Settings](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/screeners/pac/elements#indicator-settings)
    
*   [Colors](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/screeners/pac/elements#colors)
    

The Screener (OSC) supports various core features from the **Price Action Concepts®**, each listed out below.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/screeners/pac/elements#screener-elements)

Screener Elements
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Element | Description | Default |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Price | Most recent price value | Enabled |
| Volume | Most recent volume | Disabled |
| %Change | Most recent price percent change | Enabled |
| Change | Most recent price change | Disabled |
| Rating | Most recent ticker rating. The rating is given depending on the percentage of bullish information returned by all enabled screener elements for a specific ticker | Enabled |
| Structure | Most recent market structure returned on the ticker | Enabled |
| Order Block | Price position relative to the most recent Order Block area detected on the ticker | Enabled |
| Buy OB Volume | Buy volume associated to the most recently detected Order Block on the ticker | Disabled |
| Sell OB Volume | Sell volume associated to the most recently detected Order Block on the ticker | Disabled |
| OB Volume | Total volume associated to the most recently detected Order Block on the ticker | Enabled |
| Imbalances | Status of the most recent detected imbalance | Enabled |
| P&D Zones | Price position relative to the most recent premium/equilibirum/discount zones on the ticker | Disabled |
| Liquidity Grabs | Most recent detected liquidity grab | Enabled |
| EQHL | Most recent detected equal high/low | Disabled |

Each element can be disabled/enabled from the screener settings.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/screeners/pac/elements#ratings)

Ratings
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The screener ratings indicate the confluence of all returned screener data for each individual ticker by measuring the percentage of bullish indications returned by the enabled screener elements. Ratings are determined as follows:

*   ▲ Strong Bullish (more than 80% of the returned information is bullish)
*   △ Bullish (60% to 80% of the returned information is bullish)
*   ― Neutral (40% to 60% of the returned information is bullish)
*   ▽ Bearish (20% to 60% of the returned information is bullish)
*   ▼ Strong Bearish (less than 20% of the returned information is bullish)

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/screeners/pac/elements#indicator-settings)

Indicator Settings
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Users can control the settings of the included indicators in the screener from the “Indicator Settings” settings group, these include:

*   Market Structure Length
*   Order Block Length
*   Imbalance Type
*   EQHL Period

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/screeners/pac/elements#colors)

Colors
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Users are able to change the color of the information returned by each element from the “Screener Elements” settings.

YesNo

[Filtering](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/screeners/pac/filtering)

Screener Elements
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Element | Description | Default |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Price | Most recent price value | Enabled |
| Volume | Most recent volume | Disabled |
| %Change | Most recent price percent change | Enabled |
| Change | Most recent price change | Disabled |

| Reversal Zones | Current price position relative to Reversal Zones | Disabled |
| Trend Catcher | Current Trend Catcher Status | Enabled |
| Trend Tracer | Current Trend Tracer Status | Enabled |
| Neo Cloud | Current Neo Cloud Status | Disabled |
| Trend Strength | Current Trend Strength value | Enabled |
| Lux Volatility | Current Lux Volatility value | Enabled |
| Squeeze Index | Current Squeeze Index value | Enabled |

Ratings
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The screener ratings indicate the confluence of all returned screener data for each individual ticker by measuring the percentage of bullish indications returned by the enabled screener elements. Ratings are determined as follows:

*   ▲ Strong Bullish (more than 80% of the returned information is bullish)

*   ▽ Bearish (20% to 60% of the returned information is bullish)
*   ▼ Strong Bearish (less than 20% of the returned information is bullish)

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/screeners/s-o/elements#signal-settings)

Signal Settings
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The most recent signal returned by the screener is affected by the “Signal” settings group. These settings allow changing the sensitivity of the signals as well as the signal algorithm, with users having the option to select Confirmation or Contrarian signals.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/screeners/s-o/elements#overlays-settings)

Overlays Settings
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Overlay indicators screener elements are affected by their respective settings located in the “Overlays” settings group. Each overlay has an associated setting affecting their output. These settings range from 1 to 5, with higher values allowing the overlay to return indications for longer-term trends.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/screeners/s-o/elements#colors)

Colors
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Users are able to change the color of the information returned by each element from the “Screener Elements” settings.

# Intro | Alert Scripting Feature | LuxAlgo

Alert Scripting

Alert Scripting

On this page

*   [Migrations](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/alert-scripting/introduction#migrations)
    

Alert Scripting is a feature within each of our 3 exclusive toolkits that allows users to create extremely advanced alert conditions using our own scripting language. Alert Scripting is available near the bottom of the settings of each LuxAlgo toolkit, and allows using most of the features from the respective toolkits for creating alert combinations. This feature is useful for users that feel limited by the custom alert creator. To learn more about Alert Scripting, see the following pages:

Placeholders
------------

Learn how to reference market data and toolkit features when scripting alerts.

Operators
---------

Learn about the operators you can use to compare data with each other.

Actions & Methods
-----------------

Learn how to enhance scripted alerts trough actions and methods.

Usage
-----

Learn how to create simple and complex alerts.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/alert-scripting/introduction#migrations)

Migrations
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In order to migrate from older versions to more recent versions see the following page:

Migrations
----------

Migrate your script to newer version of our scripting language.

# What is TradingView? | Platform Overview | LuxAlgo

Get Started

What Is TradingView?

On this page

*   [How To Create A TradingView Account](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/getting-started/tradingview#how-to-create-a-tradingview-account)
    
*   [TradingView Charts](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/getting-started/tradingview#tradingview-charts)
    
*   [How To Open A Chart On TradingView](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/getting-started/tradingview#how-to-open-a-chart-on-tradingview)
    
*   [How To Change Symbol](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/getting-started/tradingview#how-to-change-symbol)
    
*   [Change Chart Timeframe](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/getting-started/tradingview#change-chart-timeframe)
    
*   [Add Indicators To Your Chart](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/getting-started/tradingview#add-indicators-to-your-chart)
    
*   [Save A Chart Layout](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/getting-started/tradingview#save-a-chart-layout)
    

![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/CDau_eRmDqLaKwqU/public/images/tradingview/logo-preview-2.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=CDau_eRmDqLaKwqU&q=85&s=8dcaf40a4008e1599d120d36571435bc) [TradingView](https://www.tradingview.com/)
 is a free charting platform and social network where traders/investors can **look** at financial charts and use a wide variety of tools to spot opportunity in every market across Stocks, Forex, Crypto, Futures & Commodities. TradingView users can connect most brokers to trade directly on the platform and **leap** into opportunities as they are presented in real time from their charts.

This is the platform where we host our exclusive tools. You can create a free account on TradingView and then sign up on [our website](https://luxalgo.com/pricing)
 to receive instant-access to use our tools.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/getting-started/tradingview#how-to-create-a-tradingview-account)

How To Create A TradingView Account
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In order to create a TradingView account, you need to go to the TradingView [homepage](https://www.tradingview.com/)
. Click on “Sign in” at the top right of the homepage, then click on “Sign up” at the bottom of the current window. You can sign up using your social media profiles or an email address. ![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/CDau_eRmDqLaKwqU/public/images/tradingview/image581.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=CDau_eRmDqLaKwqU&q=85&s=64d2f214808903029701207cef17c1ff) ![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/CDau_eRmDqLaKwqU/public/images/tradingview/image637.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=CDau_eRmDqLaKwqU&q=85&s=252154cae6ada54e0eda0e3c69a86659)

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/getting-started/tradingview#tradingview-charts)

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/getting-started/tradingview#how-to-change-symbol)

How To Change Symbol

![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/CDau_eRmDqLaKwqU/public/images/tradingview/image50.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=CDau_eRmDqLaKwqU&q=85&s=8c37ae11a52b8ad6428938c07658279f) You can change the symbol of the chart by clicking on the top left section containing the current chart ticker.

Once you click on it, you will be able to search for specific symbols. ###

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/getting-started/tradingview#save-a-chart-layout)

Save A Chart Layout

You can create, delete and save chart layouts on TradingView if you wish to save your indicator & chart settings on specific tickers/timeframes. Once you make a change on a layout, you will need to save these changes, all you need to do is to click on the cloud symbol at the top right of the chart. ![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/CDau_eRmDqLaKwqU/public/images/tradingview/image356.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=CDau_eRmDqLaKwqU&q=85&s=a78d65b66667f0b6ce0b115ff249b49a) ![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/CDau_eRmDqLaKwqU/public/images/tradingview/image225.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=CDau_eRmDqLaKwqU&q=85&s=9a98168ca24774defdac448374e7acad)

You can also save a chart layout by pressing `ctrl + s` or `cmd + s` for mac users, on your keyboard.

# Take Profit & Stop Losses | Backtester (S&O) | LuxAlgo

[Skip to main content](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-backtesting/backtesters/s-o/tpsl#content-area)

[LuxAlgo home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=9a82ae47268cbdb594f7f904c8dc654f)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=9db2e704694ba3dd9d249afa92f16cc5)](https://docs.luxalgo.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Backtester (S&O)

Take Profit & Stop Loss

On this page

*   [TP/SL Options](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-backtesting/backtesters/s-o/tpsl#tp%2Fsl-options)
    
*   [Trailing Stop](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-backtesting/backtesters/s-o/tpsl#trailing-stop)
    
*   [Take Profits Levels From Forecast](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-backtesting/backtesters/s-o/tpsl#take-profits-levels-from-forecast)
    

![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/backtesters/tpsl.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=03c79b3c5ccb64009becd8e7501485c9) Users can set take profits and stop losses orders allowing a certain degree of money management in the backtest. Take profits and stop loss orders can be enabled and adjusted from the **FIXED TPS & SLS** settings section.

Take profits and stop losses orders are placed relative to the price preceding a trade, and might not be filled at the exact price set by the user.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-backtesting/backtesters/s-o/tpsl#tp/sl-options)

TP/SL Options
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Take profits and stop losses for specific orders can be enabled from the toggles in their settings section. Take profits and stop losses can be set using various methods described below:

| Option | Description |
| --- | --- |
| Price | Set the take profit/stop loss orders at the specified price. |
| Currency | Set the take profit/stop loss orders a specified amount of currency away from the closing price preceding the entry of a long/short order. |
| Ticks | Set the take profit/stop loss orders a specified amount of ticks away from the closing price preceding the entry of a long/short order. |
| %   | Set the take profit/stop loss orders a specified percentage away from the closing price preceding the entry of a long/short order. |
| ATR | Set the take profit/stop loss orders _N_ average true ranges away from the closing price preceding the entry of a long/short order, where _N_ is a specified multiplier. |
| Forecast | (Only available for take profits orders) Use a percentile of a returned forecast to set take profits. Forecasts must be enabled in order for this to work. |
| Trailing Stop | (Only available for stop loss orders) Enable a percentage-based trailing stop. A position will be exited if the price reaches the trailing stop. |

The average true range used to set take profits/stop losses orders uses a period of 200 bars.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-backtesting/backtesters/s-o/tpsl#trailing-stop)

Trailing Stop

![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/backtesters/trailing.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=c724c49ece0d25fce812a91dc50e5d29) Users can use a percentage-based trailing stop to exit positions. The trailing stop will move in the direction of interest if its distance with the low price (in case of long positions) or high price (in case of short positions) is greater than the specified percentage.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/ai-backtesting/backtesters/s-o/tpsl#take-profits-levels-from-forecast)

Take Profits Levels From Forecast

When forecasts are displayed, users can set take profits using the **nth** percentile of a returned forecast. This can be done from the “TPS & SLS” settings, by selecting “Forecast” in the “Long TP” and/or “Short TP”. The numerical setting selected at the right of the drop-down menus determines the percentile used, and should be set within the range \[0, 100\] in order to work. Percentiles values can affect the returned levels as follows:

*   In case of a long trade, a lower set percentile will return take profits closer to the entry price, potentially triggering sooner.
*   In case of a short trade, a lower set percentile will return take profits further away from the entry price, potentially triggering later.

Do note that because forecasts are based on the strategy entries, take profits levels based on it can be subject to repainting, except when using a backtesting window based on a date.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

Oscillator Matrix

Reversal Signals

On this page

*   [Classification](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/reversal-signals#classification)
    

![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/fwDpVLIFpofJkOq8/public/images/lux-oscillator/reversal-signals/settings.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=fwDpVLIFpofJkOq8&q=85&s=6fef7af8e90de8aa83d3d7b3071d1b98)

Classification
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/fwDpVLIFpofJkOq8/public/images/lux-oscillator/reversal-signals/reversals.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=fwDpVLIFpofJkOq8&q=85&s=06e3f044ad10d28fb4385b06632ab2be) Different kind of reversals are returned on the oscillators pane, minor (-) and major (+) reversals signals. Minor reversals are frequent signals often indicative of shorter term reversals, such as the top/bottom of an impulse (thus announcing a retracement). Minor reversals are highlighted by circles. Major reversals can occur later in a trend, and can be indicative of a more significant reversals. Major reversals are highlighted by triangles.

# Confluence | Oscillator Matrix | LuxAlgo

[Skip to main content](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/confluence#content-area)

[LuxAlgo home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=9a82ae47268cbdb594f7f904c8dc654f)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=9db2e704694ba3dd9d249afa92f16cc5)](https://docs.luxalgo.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Oscillator Matrix

Confluence

On this page

*   [Confluence Zones](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/confluence#confluence-zones)
    
*   [Confluence Meter](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/confluence#confluence-meter)
    

![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/fwDpVLIFpofJkOq8/public/images/lux-oscillator/confluence/settings.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=fwDpVLIFpofJkOq8&q=85&s=35bbe83ee71482761ed113e1c6e81fe0)

Confluence is an important aspect when dealing with multiple indicators. In this toolkit two features allows the users to easily assess if the confluence between each toolkit element in high or low.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/confluence#confluence-zones)

Confluence Zones
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/fwDpVLIFpofJkOq8/public/images/lux-oscillator/confluence/zones.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=fwDpVLIFpofJkOq8&q=85&s=539ca3ab6cf1182c1d9eeb9603ade1e8) Users can see on the oscillators pane one upper (above 100) and lower (under 0) zone, measuring the bullish/bearish confluence between the Hyper Wave and Money Flow oscillators. When both the Hyper Wave and Money Flow oscillators are indicating an uptrend the upper zone is colored with a darker green. If only one of the oscillators is indicating an uptrend then the confluence zone will have a brighter green. This logic applies to the lower zone in the case of a downtrend.

Confluence zones have an associated numerical that can be used in external scripts using the output “Upper Confluence Value” for the upper confluence zone and “Lower Confluence Value” for the lower confluence zone, returned values include:

*   2: Strong confluence
*   1: Weak confluence
*   0: No confluence

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/confluence#confluence-meter)

Confluence Meter
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/fwDpVLIFpofJkOq8/public/images/lux-oscillator/confluence/meter.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=fwDpVLIFpofJkOq8&q=85&s=1643146e249c5dd986498e07eaa89158) The confluence meter quantifies the amount of confluence between each indication returned by the oscillator, elements taken into account are:

*   Trend indicated by the Hyper Wave relative to its signal line
*   Trend indicated by the Hyper Wave
*   Trend indicated by the Money Flow
*   Overflow
*   Divergences

The meter giving a higher measurement would be indicative of a more significant bullish confluence, that is most elements are indicative of a bullish trend, while a lower measurement would be indicative of a more significant bearish confluence.

The confluence meter had an associated numerical that can be used in external scripts using the output “Confluence Meter Value”

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

Screener (PAC)

Sorting

On this page

*   [Structure Sorting](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/screeners/pac/sorting#structure-sorting)
    
*   [Structure (Absolute) Sorting](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/screeners/pac/sorting#structure-absolute-sorting)
    

![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/CDau_eRmDqLaKwqU/public/images/screeners/sort.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=CDau_eRmDqLaKwqU&q=85&s=86177b3816265d7a3b2beeee79752468) Users can sort certain elements returning/or with associated numerical information in either a descending or ascending order. This can be useful to see specific tickers first or last depending on the sorted data on the screener. Supported elements for sorting include:

*   Rating
*   Structure
*   Structure (Absolute)
*   OB Volume
*   OB Buy Volume
*   OB Sell Volume
*   None

When “None” is selected the screener tickers appear as per their order in the Tickers settings.

![Tickers sorted by rating in a descending order](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-_VCBHd2xJR0PihX/public/images/screeners/osc/sorting/sorted.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=-_VCBHd2xJR0PihX&q=85&s=dda7bbe9e63036141d0c0eb57c7f3afa)

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/screeners/pac/sorting#structure-sorting)

Structure Sorting
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

By default, sorting by **Structure** orders rows from the strongest **bearish** structures to the strongest **bullish** ones (and inversely if “Ascending” is toggled on). The ranking used, from strongest to weakest, is:

*   Higher consecutive BOS
*   CHoCH+
*   CHoCH

This same ranking is applied in both bearish and bullish directions.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/screeners/pac/sorting#structure-absolute-sorting)

Structure (Absolute) Sorting

The **Structure (Absolute)** option ignores the direction (bullish or bearish) and sorts all structures purely based on the previous ranking.

# What is LuxAlgo? | AI Strategy Platform | LuxAlgo

[Skip to main content](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/getting-started/what-is-luxalgo#content-area)

[LuxAlgo home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=9a82ae47268cbdb594f7f904c8dc654f)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=9db2e704694ba3dd9d249afa92f16cc5)](https://docs.luxalgo.com/)

Search...

Get Started

What Is LuxAlgo?

On this page

*   [Architect Your Edge](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/getting-started/what-is-luxalgo#architect-your-edge)
    
*   [From Indicators to Intelligence](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/getting-started/what-is-luxalgo#from-indicators-to-intelligence)
    
*   [The LuxAlgo Advantage](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/getting-started/what-is-luxalgo#the-luxalgo-advantage)
    
*   [Why LuxAlgo AI Beats Generic Models](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/getting-started/what-is-luxalgo#why-luxalgo-ai-beats-generic-models)
    

LuxAlgo is the leading AI platform for generating indicators and trading strategies. We are widely known for hosting the world’s largest open-source [Library](https://luxalgo.com/library)
 of trading indicators & algorithms used by millions of traders across 5+ charting platforms such as TradingView, however, this massive repository serves a higher purpose. It acts as the intelligence engine that powers our advanced AI platform for indicators and strategy creation. We constantly automate technical analysis concepts traders use into scripts, innovate on them by building advanced algorithms, and package all of them into a streamlined AI platform. An ecosystem where traders can easily generate smarter, statistically robust strategies of their own rather than relying on someone elses research or market “edge”. ![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/CDau_eRmDqLaKwqU/public/images/what-is-luxalgo/what-is-luxalgo.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=CDau_eRmDqLaKwqU&q=85&s=81dcb0ad15be334fa9ac45073d26fdb2)

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/getting-started/what-is-luxalgo#architect-your-edge)

Architect Your Edge
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Quant is our AI coding agent specialized in generating and validating Pine Script® indicators and strategies for TradingView®. Built on our extensive library of proprietary tools and frameworks, Quant transforms your trading ideas into production-ready code. Whether you’re describing an indicator concept in plain language or uploading a chart screenshot, Quant leverages deep Pine Script® knowledge to architect, validate, and deploy custom trading tools instantly—no coding experience required.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/getting-started/what-is-luxalgo#from-indicators-to-intelligence)

From Indicators to Intelligence
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

LuxAlgo transforms the traditional concept of a “trading library” into an active strategy engine. While most platforms provide disconnected tools that require users to manually guess which settings or combinations might work, our platform automates this complexity. We utilize the vast logic within our proprietary toolkits to serve as the foundation for **automated strategy generation**.

*   **Automated Discovery:** Instead of manually testing hundreds of settings, our engine iterates through them to find statistically significant setups.
*   **Data-Driven Decisions:** Strategies are built on concrete historical data from our advanced toolkits, not subjective chart reading.
*   **Optimization:** The platform identifies the specific parameters that have historically aligned with market movements, removing the need for random trial and error.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/getting-started/what-is-luxalgo#the-luxalgo-advantage)

The LuxAlgo Advantage
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Our advantage comes from the quality of the data feeding our platform. LuxAlgo is the only company with a proprietary library deep enough to train a specialized trading engine effectively. The logic driving our platform is validated by the world’s largest community of technical traders. Our underlying algorithms are used by **over 1 million followers** on TradingView and are developed by a team holding the rare **‘Pine Wizard’** distinction. This means the strategies you generate aren’t based on generic code, but on the highest-rated, most stress-tested technical trading concepts in the world.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/getting-started/what-is-luxalgo#why-luxalgo-ai-beats-generic-models)

Why LuxAlgo AI Beats Generic Models
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

A common question is: _“Can’t I just use ChatGPT or generic AI to make an indicator or trading strategy myself?”_ Generic AI models (LLMs) cannot access specialized data & tools for building strategies on their own. They lack the structured environment required to build executable trading systems and often will just give you bug-filled, outdated, irrelevant Pine Script code for TradingView. This is often seen with generic LLMs LuxAlgo is backed by **proprietary trading intelligence** that generic AI lacks:

1.  **Structured Framework:** Unlike a chatbot that writes theoretical code, LuxAlgo’s AI operates within a rigorous testing environment using our proprietary Signal & Overlay™ and Price Action™ architectures.
2.  **No Hallucinations:** Our platform doesn’t “invent” data. It iterates through actual, hard-coded parameters within our algorithmic trading tools to find what is mathematically valid.
3.  **Actionable Output:** While a generic AI might give you a vague concept, LuxAlgo delivers a fully configured, backtested strategy ready to be deployed immediately.

Oscillator Matrix

Introduction

On this page

*   [Features](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/introduction#features)
    
*   [Alerts](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/introduction#alerts)
    
*   [Settings Reference](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/introduction#settings-reference)
    

Oscillator Matrix® is an all-in-one indicator that incorporates 6+ unique components designed for interoperability & confluence with one another to provide a powerful trend following & reversal detection experience. Users can create various ways to utilize the indicator’s features together such as looking for excess money flowing into the market alongside strong reversal signals appearing, or getting real-time divergence signals alongside a lack of money flowing into the market to predict upcoming trends. This indicator is described as an ‘Oscillator Matrix’ as it’s made up of many different components that can create a systematic approach to analyzing markets alone, however, the indicator also can serve as a great secondary piece to a user’s primary analysis with or without our other LuxAlgo Premium indicators.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/introduction#features)

HyperWave
---------

Smart Money Flow
----------------

----------------

Confluence
----------

# Smart Money Flow | Oscillator Matrix | LuxAlgo

[Skip to main content](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/smart-money-flow#content-area)

[LuxAlgo home page![light logo](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/logo/light.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=9a82ae47268cbdb594f7f904c8dc654f)![dark logo](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/logo/dark.png?fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=9db2e704694ba3dd9d249afa92f16cc5)](https://docs.luxalgo.com/)

Search...

⌘KAsk AI

Search...

Navigation

Oscillator Matrix

Smart Money Flow

On this page

*   [Money Flow](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/smart-money-flow#money-flow)
    
*   [Overflow](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/smart-money-flow#overflow)
    
*   [Money Flow Thresholds](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/smart-money-flow#money-flow-thresholds)
    

![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/fwDpVLIFpofJkOq8/public/images/lux-oscillator/smart-money-flow/settings.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=fwDpVLIFpofJkOq8&q=85&s=0a5fe6230fbe823536a4c1d3e45c34f1)

Money Flow and liquidity are core concepts with the Oscillator Matrix®. Various elements centered around this concept are provided to detect longer term trends, assess market participants behaviours, and detect reversals.

The Money Flow and every associated components (overflow, thresholds) can be disabled by toggling off “Show Money Flow”

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/smart-money-flow#money-flow)

Money Flow
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/fwDpVLIFpofJkOq8/public/images/lux-oscillator/smart-money-flow/money-flow.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=fwDpVLIFpofJkOq8&q=85&s=3d91870d876150244634fa04031e9f44) The toolkit include one money flow indicator that aims to detect trends based on market participants activity. Compared to the Hyper Wave the Money Flow oscillator can return longer term indications and be used to support shorter term indications.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/smart-money-flow#overflow)

Overflow
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/fwDpVLIFpofJkOq8/public/images/lux-oscillator/smart-money-flow/overflow.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=fwDpVLIFpofJkOq8&q=85&s=e638aac83b5e88f665bc8bc3d9f3f778) Overflow occurs when excessive liquidity relative to a trend length enters the market, this can highlight late trend following participants entering the market, and can announce potential reversals.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/smart-money-flow#money-flow-thresholds)

Money Flow Thresholds

![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/fwDpVLIFpofJkOq8/public/images/lux-oscillator/smart-money-flow/thresholds.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=fwDpVLIFpofJkOq8&q=85&s=7193bd3279902375f8e693bc5a57c865) Users can gauge market activity by using the provided Money Flow thresholds, two extremities displayed above/under the central 50 levels. When the Money Flow oscillator is above the upper threshold there is significant one-sided bullish activity on the market. When the Money Flow oscillator is under the lower threshold there is significant one-sided bearish activity on the market. Money flow fluctuating within the thresholds can highlight a more balanced market.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

[HyperWave](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/hyperwave)
[Reversal Signals](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/reversal-signals)

Screener (OSC)

Introduction

On this page

*   [Tickers](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/screeners/osc/introduction#tickers)
    
*   [Display](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/screeners/osc/introduction#display)
    
*   [Notes](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/screeners/osc/introduction#notes)
    
*   [Computation](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/screeners/osc/introduction#computation)
    
*   [Inconsistency](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/screeners/osc/introduction#inconsistency)
    

![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-_VCBHd2xJR0PihX/public/images/screeners/osc/introduction/screener.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=-_VCBHd2xJR0PihX&q=85&s=adf883cdc4d47cc021b89a35ffa9a899) The Screener (OSC) is a useful tool able to return recent information from various features in the **Oscillator Matrix®** toolkit for up to 10 user set tickers with customizable timeframe. In order to use the screener the best way possible it is first advised to fully understand the [Oscillator Matrix®](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/introduction)
 toolkit.

Provided below are pages describing all key features included.

Elements
--------

Filtering
---------

Sorting
-------

Having access to the **Oscillator Matrix®** will automatically grant you access to the OSC screener.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/screeners/osc/introduction#tickers)

Tickers
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Users can change tickers as well as their respective timeframes from the screener settings. Default tickers include:

*   BTCUSDT
*   ETHUSDT
*   SOLUSDT
*   ADAUSDT
*   SPX
*   AAPL
*   TSLA
*   NVDA
*   EURUSD
*   GBPUSD

The default timeframe used for all is the user chart timeframe. Supported tickers includes all tickers available on Tradingview (note that this availability can be affected by your Tradingview plan). Users can also use the same ticker but different timeframes, allowing to perform multi timeframe analysis of the **Oscillator Matrix®** toolkit. However, duplicated tickers with the same timeframe will result in the duplicate ticker to not appear on the screener.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/screeners/osc/introduction#display)

Display
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Users are offered a high degree of freedom when it comes to the placement of the screener. By default, the screener is located on a different pane, with the options to select the following positions:

*   Top Center
*   Top Right
*   Top Left
*   Bottom Center
*   Bottom Right
*   Bottom Left

It is also common for more compact screeners to be directly on the price chart, this is possible with this screener by drag and dropping it to the user chart, or by moving it to the existing pane above assuming the screener is in a pane below the price chart. ![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-_VCBHd2xJR0PihX/public/images/screeners/pane.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=-_VCBHd2xJR0PihX&q=85&s=44d65f4c4c11edffb6d582b8717b402d)

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/screeners/osc/introduction#notes)

Notes
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Tradingview is not a friendly environment when it comes to running more complete screeners, this cause various limitations showcased below:

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/screeners/osc/introduction#computation)

Computation

The computation of a screener on Tradingview is very intensive, as such you can expect rare calculations timeouts. When this occurs simply force the screener recalculation by modifying one setting or adding the screener again to your chart.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/screeners/osc/introduction#inconsistency)

Inconsistency

It is possible to observe inconsistencies when observing the screener on a chart with a specific symbol due to screener tickers having being on different market. The crypto market operates 24/7 while stock markets have opening and closing times, this can cause the screener to return different information when observing it from a cryptocurrency or stock/currency pair.

Get Started

FAQ

On this page

*   [Access](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/getting-started/faq#access)
    
*   [Products](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/getting-started/faq#products)
