The Price Action Concepts® can alert users for multiple events relevant to the existing features in the toolkit. To learn more about how to set alerts in general see [how to create alerts on tradingview](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/getting-started/tradingview-alerts)
.

In order for an alert to work in the toolkit make sure the related feature is enabled

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/alerts#any-alert-function-call)

Any Alert() Function Call
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Users can create a single alert for multiple conditions using the _any alert() function call_ alert condition. Conditions users want to be alerted for are grouped by the type of features they affect (structures, volumetric order blocks, imbalances…etc) and are located at the bottom of the toolkit settings. Once conditions are toggled on users only need to set an alert using the _any alert() function call_ as condition. ![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/fwDpVLIFpofJkOq8/public/images/lux-pa/alerts/set.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=fwDpVLIFpofJkOq8&q=85&s=f302920dbab26ae81d7d95bf3826f4f5)

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/alerts#any-alert-function-call-message)

Any Alert() Function Call Message

Users can set a custom message that will be used when an any alert() function call condition is triggered in the message field below the list of conditions. Users can use placeholders to customize messages and return useful information, the following placeholders are supported:

#### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/alerts#symbol-placeholders)

Symbol Placeholders

| Placeholder | Description | Example |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `{default}` | Default message associated with the trigerred condition | `"Mitigated Bullish Imbalance"` |
| `{ticker}` | Symbol ticker without the exchange prefix | `"MSFT"` |
| `{exchange}` | Symbol exchange/data source | `"COINBASE"` |
| `{sector}` | Sector of the symbol, `na` if the symbol has no sector | `"Technology Services"` |
| `{market}` | Symbol market type | `"Stocks"` |

#### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/alerts#time-placeholders)

Time Placeholders

| Placeholder | Description | Example |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `{tf}` | Chart timeframe, includes “S” for seconds, “D” for days, “W” for weeks, “M” for months | `"15"` |
| `{time}` | Unix time in milliseconds in exchange timezone | `"1705331385158"` |
| `{year}` | Current year in exchange timezone | `"2024"` |
| `{month}` | Current month in exchange timezone | `"7"` |
| `{day}` | Current day of the month in exchange timezone | `"21"` |

#### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/alerts#data-placeholders)

Data Placeholders

| Placeholder | Description | Example |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `{open}` | Opening price | `"1.2145"` |
| `{high}` | High price | `"1.2357"` |
| `{low}` | Low price | `"1.1983"` |
| `{close}` | Closing price | `"1.0569"` |
| `{volume}` | Current volume | `"45216"` |
| `{ob_buy_volume}` | Most recent order block internal buy volume | `"560"` |
| `{ob_sell_volume}` | Most recent order block internal sell volume | `"480"` |
| `{ob_volume}` | Most recent order block total internal volume | `"1040"` |

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/alerts#format-as-json)

Format as JSON

Use the following message template to receive “any alert() function call” messages in the JSON format:

    {
      "alert": "{default}",
      "ticker": "{ticker}",
      "tf": "{tf}",
      "ohlcv":{
        "open": {open},
        "high": {high},
        "low": {low},
        "close": {close},
        "volume": {volume},
        "order block buy volume": {ob_buy_volume},
        "order block sell volume": {ob_sell_volume},
        "order block total volume": {ob_volume}
      },
      "bartime": {time}
    }
    

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/alerts#custom-alert-creator)

Custom Alert Creator
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/fwDpVLIFpofJkOq8/public/images/lux-pa/alerts/custom.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=fwDpVLIFpofJkOq8&q=85&s=9f3ac70c3f16520e032288c0928db8f3) Users wishing to construct more complex alerts using features within the toolkit and/or external indicators can use the **Custom Alert Creator**. The custom alert creator allows alerting when various user-set conditions are met or when a sequence of conditions is complete.

A user wishing to be alerted when any internal market structure occurs within 1AM and 5AM of the symbol timezone could do it as follows:![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/fwDpVLIFpofJkOq8/public/images/lux-pa/alerts/custom_example.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=fwDpVLIFpofJkOq8&q=85&s=b17886a3bdf43fb92807e8ac577e8fbb)

A custom alert can be triggered as an _any alert() function call_ if the setting is selected or as a regular alert when selected in the Tradingview alert creator menu.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/alerts#steps)

Steps

Steps allow creating a sequence of conditions, which when met trigger an alert. When a condition with a step equal to 1 is met the next condition associated with step 2 will be evaluated (if enabled) and so on for higher steps (if any). Conditions with the same associated step will require both conditions to be true in order for the condition associated with a higher step (if any) to be evaluated. This allows certain conditions to act as filters.

A user wishing to be alerted when the price enters a bullish imbalance after any internal bullish market structure could do it as follows:![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/fwDpVLIFpofJkOq8/public/images/lux-pa/alerts/step_example.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=fwDpVLIFpofJkOq8&q=85&s=a454dffca1cee9d66853f33977b480ef)_Make sure internal market structures and imbalances are enabled_.

Make sure steps are set such that they form a linear sequence. For example, if the lowest step is 2 or if the set steps are only 1 and 3 an error will be returned.

#### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/alerts#or-step-operator)

OR Step Operator

The “OR” step operator can be used to get alerted for any additional condition using “OR” as a step, in addition to other set custom alert conditions. Conditions using the “OR” step can be highlighted using a different color, which can be set from the Custom Alert Creator settings. Users can choose the location of this visual element (top or bottom of the chart).

#### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/alerts#all-step-operator)

All Step Operator

The “All” step operator can be used to filter any set “Step” condition, including “OR” and “Invalidate”. This step operator can be useful if all the steps in a sequence needs to obey a specific rule.

If a user has 2 steps set, and requires both of these to occur at a specific time interval such as 9am to 1pm, then we can use a “Session” condition using the “All” step, requiring our step 1 and step 2 to be occur between 9am and 1pm.

#### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/alerts#invalidate-step)

Invalidate Step

The “Invalidate” step allows to set a condition as an “invalidation condition”. When this condition is triggered while a sequence of conditions is incomplete, the sequence will restart at step 1. If multiple steps are set as “Invalidate” any of the conditions being true will reset the sequence of conditions, as such not all of them are required to be true for the sequence of conditions to reset.

Example
-------

Let’s take an example where we use 2 regular steps and one “Invalidate” step. The alert will trigger when step 2 trigger after step 1 has been triggered.

1

[](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/alerts#)

Step 1

Step 1 condition trigger, we will now evaluate step 2 from now on.

2

[](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/alerts#)

Invalidation Step

Invalidation step condition trigger, we reset the sequence and evaluate step 1 just after.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/alerts#invalidation-behaviors)

Invalidation Behaviors

Invalidation behaviors allows adding more restrictions to a sequence of conditions, users can use two different invalidation behaviors described below:

#### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/alerts#invalidate-on-step-1)

Invalidate On Step 1

The “Invalidate On Step 1” behavior allows to reset an incomplete sequence of conditions when the condition on step 1 trigger. This prevents the first step condition from happening in between other steps of the condition sequence. This behavior is useful when the first step of our sequence of conditions needs to never be repeated during the sequence.

Example
-------

Let’s take an example where we use 3 regular steps.

1

[](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/alerts#)

Step 1

Step 1 condition trigger, we will now evaluate step 2 from now on.

2

[](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/alerts#)

Step 2

Step 2 condition trigger, we will now evaluate step 3 from now on.

3

[](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/alerts#)

Step 1 Trigger

Step 1 condition trigger, we start evaluating step 2 from now.

#### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/alerts#invalidate-on-any-repeated-step)

Invalidate On Any Repeated Step

The “Invalidate On Any Repeated Step” behavior allows to reset an incomplete sequence of conditions when a step is triggered such that it does not respect the set order of conditions. This behavior is useful when we want a perfectly ordered sequence of conditions to complete, without any step repeating itself.

Example
-------

Let’s take an example where we use 3 regular steps.

1

[](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/alerts#)

Step 1

Step 1 condition trigger, we will now evaluate step 2 from now on.

2

[](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/alerts#)

Step 2

Step 2 condition trigger, we will now evaluate step 3 from now on.

3

[](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/alerts#)

Step 1 or 2 Trigger

Step 1 or 2 conditions trigger, we start evaluating step 1 from now.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/alerts#maximum-step-interval)

Maximum Step Interval

Users can determine what is the maximum allowed horizontal distance (in bars) between two steps by enabling the “Maximum Step Interval” setting. This allows restricting steps separated by a large amount of bars. If the amount of bars since a step exceed the set threshold, then the conditions sequence is reset, and we start evaluating from step 1 again.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/alerts#highlight-on-chart)

Highlight On Chart

When a custom alert condition is set, a visual element is displayed at the bottom of the chart in order to more easily visualize when the custom alert condition occurs (displayed by default).

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/alerts#alerts-reference)

Alerts Reference
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/alerts#pre-set-alerts)

Pre-Set Alerts

| Alert | Description |
| --- | --- |
| Bullish I-BOS | Triggers on the event of an internal bullish break of structure (BOS) |
| Bullish I-CHOCH | Triggers on the event of an internal bullish change of character (CHOCH) |
| Bullish I-CHOCH+ | Triggers on the event of a Supported internal bullish change of character (CHOCH+) |
| Bearish I-BOS | Triggers on the event of an internal bearish break of structure (BOS) |
| Bearish I-CHOCH | Triggers on the event of an internal bearish change of character (CHOCH) |
| Bearish I-CHOCH+ | Triggers on the event of a Supported internal bearish change of character (CHOCH+) |
| Bullish S-BOS | Triggers on the event of a swing bullish break of structure (BOS) |
| Bullish S-CHOCH | Triggers on the event of a swing bullish change of character (CHOCH) |
| Bullish S-CHOCH+ | Triggers on the event of a Supported swing bullish change of character (CHOCH+) |
| Bearish S-BOS | Triggers on the event of a swing bearish break of structure (BOS) |
| Bearish S-CHOCH | Triggers on the event of a swing bearish change of character (CHOCH) |
| Bearish S-CHOCH+ | Triggers on the event of a Supported swing bearish change of character (CHOCH+) |
| Equal Highs | Triggers on the event of an equal high (EQH) |
| Equal Lows | Triggers on the event of an equal low (EQL) |
| Bullish OB Created | Triggers when a new bullish order block is created |
| Bearish OB Created | Triggers when a new bearish order block is created |
| Bullish OB Mitigated | Triggers when a bullish order block (visible or not) is mitigated |
| Bearish OB Mitigated | Triggers when a bearish order block (visible or not) is mitigated |
| Bullish Breaker | Triggers when a bullish order block (visible or not) becomes a breaker block |
| Bearish Breaker | Triggers when a bearish order block (visible or not) becomes a breaker block |
| Within Bullish OB | Triggers when the price is located within a bullish order block (visible or not) |
| Within Bearish OB | Triggers when the price is located within a bearish order block (visible or not) |
| Bullish OB Entered | Triggers when the price enters a bullish order block (visible or not) |
| Bearish OB Entered | Triggers when the price enters a bearish order block (visible or not) |
| Bullish Imbalance | Triggers when a new bullish imbalance is detected |
| Bearish Imbalance | Triggers when a new bearish imbalance is detected |
| Bullish Imbalance Mitigated | Triggers when a bullish imbalance (visible or not) is mitigated |
| Bearish Imbalance Mitigated | Triggers when a bearish imbalance (visible or not) is mitigated |
| Broken Uptrendline | Triggers when an upward trendline is broken |
| Broken Downtrendline | Triggers when a downward trendline is broken |
| Bullish Grab | Triggers when a new bullish liquidity grab is detected |
| Bearish Grab | Triggers when a new bearish liquidity grab is detected |
| Custom Alert Condition | Triggers on the event of a user set custom alert condition being true |

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/alerts#any-alert-function-call-2)

Any alert() Function Call

* * *

#### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/alerts#custom-alert-creator-2)

Custom Alert Creator

| Alert | Description | Default |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Trigger as any alert() function call | Triggers on the event of a user set custom alert condition being true |     |

#### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/alerts#market-structures)

Market Structures

| Alert | Description | Default |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Bullish I-BOS | Triggers on the event of an internal bullish break of structure (BOS) |     |
| Swing BOS | Triggers on the event of a swing bullish break of structure (BOS) |     |
| Bearish I-BOS | Triggers on the event of an internal bearish break of structure (BOS) |     |
| Swing BOS | Triggers on the event of a swing bearish break of structure (BOS) |     |
| Bullish I-CHOCH | Triggers on the event of an internal bullish change of character (CHOCH) |     |
| Swing CHOCH | Triggers on the event of a swing bullish change of character (CHOCH) |     |
| Bullish I-CHOCH+ | Triggers on the event of a Supported internal bullish change of character (CHOCH+) |     |
| Swing CHOCH+ | Triggers on the event of a Supported swing bullish change of character (CHOCH+) |     |
| Bearish I-CHOCH | Triggers on the event of an internal bearish change of character (CHOCH) |     |
| Swing CHOCH | Triggers on the event of a swing bearish change of character (CHOCH) |     |
| Bearish I-CHOCH+ | Triggers on the event of a Supported internal bearish change of character (CHOCH+) |     |
| Swing CHOCH+ | Triggers on the event of a Supported swing bearish change of character (CHOCH+) |     |

#### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/alerts#volumetric-order-blocks)

Volumetric Order Blocks

| Alert | Description | Default |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Bullish OB | Triggers when a new bullish order block is created |     |
| Bearish OB | Triggers when a new bearish order block is created |     |
| Bullish OB Mitigated | Triggers when a bullish order block (visible or not) is mitigated |     |
| Bearish OB Mitigated | Triggers when a bearish order block (visible or not) is mitigated |     |
| Bullish Breaker | Triggers when a bullish order block (visible or not) becomes a breaker block |     |
| Bearish Breaker | Triggers when a bearish order block (visible or not) becomes a breaker block |     |
| Within Bullish OB | Triggers when the price is located within a bullish order block (visible or not) |     |
| Within Bearish OB | Triggers when the price is located within a bearish order block (visible or not) |     |
| Bullish OB Entered | Triggers when the price enters a bullish order block (visible or not) |     |
| Bearish OB Entered | Triggers when the price enters a bearish order block (visible or not) |     |
| Bullish OB Exited | Triggers when the price exits a bullish order block |     |
| Bearish OB Exited | Triggers when the price exits a bearish order block |     |

#### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/alerts#imbalances)

Imbalances

| Alert | Description | Default |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Any New Imbalance | Triggers when a bullish or bearish imbalance is identified |     |
| Bullish New Imbalance | Triggers when a bullish imbalance is identified |     |
| Bearish New Imbalance | Triggers when a bearish imbalance is identified |     |
| Any Imbalance Mitigated | Triggers when a bullish or bearish imbalance is mitigated |     |
| Bullish Imbalance Mitigated | Triggers when a bullish imbalance is mitigated |     |
| Bearish Imbalance Mitigated | Triggers when a bearish imbalance is mitigated |     |
| Within Any Imbalance | Triggers when the price is located within a bullish or bearish imbalance |     |
| Within Bullish Imbalance | Triggers when the price is located within a bullish imbalance |     |
| Within Bearish Imbalance | Triggers when the price is located within a bearish imbalance |     |
| Any Imbalance Entered | Triggers when the price enters a bullish or bearish imbalance |     |
| Bullish Imbalance Entered | Triggers when the price enters a bullish imbalance |     |
| Bearish Imbalance Entered | Triggers when the price enters a bearish imbalance |     |
| Bullish Imbalance Exited | Triggers when the price exits a bullish imbalance |     |
| Bearish Imbalance Exited | Triggers when the price exits a bearish imbalance |     |

#### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/alerts#liquidity-concepts)

Liquidity Concepts

| Alert | Description | Default |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Up-Trendline Break | Triggers when the price breaks above an upward trendline |     |
| Down-Trendline Break | Triggers when the price breaks below a downward trendline |     |
| Detected Pattern | Triggers when a user-set chart pattern is identified |     |
| Equal High | Triggers when a new equal high is detected |     |
| Equal Low | Triggers when a new equal low is detected |     |
| Bullish Grab | Triggers when a bullish liquidity grab occurs |     |
| Bearish Grab | Triggers when a bearish liquidity grab occurs |     |

Signals & Overlays® can alert users for multiple events relevant to the existing features in the toolkit. To learn more about how to set alerts in general see [how to create alerts on tradingview](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/getting-started/tradingview-alerts)
.

In order for an alert to work in the toolkit make sure the related feature is enabled

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/alerts#using-placeholders-with-confirmation/contrarian-alerts)

Using Placeholders With Confirmation/Contrarian Alerts
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/lux-algo/alerts/image620.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=6a0d328d46728bbef8481a74b86f1af7) When creating an alert using ‘Any Confirmation’ or ‘Any Contrarian’ it is possible to use placeholders so that the alert message returns the type of signal that triggered the alert. In order to do so, paste the following line in the message field:

    Bullish : {{plot("Bullish")}} | Bearish : {{plot("Bearish")}} | Bullish+: {{plot("Bullish+")}} | Bearish+ : {{plot("Bearish+")}}
    

![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/lux-algo/alerts/image31.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=bddf8337ff55e2cdabf8acca9f8003d2)

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/alerts#any-alert-function-call)

Any Alert() Function Call
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The _any alert() function call_ alert condition allows to create one alert using various conditions, this allows to bypass the limit of one alert for free users as well as making the process of updating many alerts faster and easier. To create such an alert go to the indicator settings, and scroll down to the ‘**ANY ALERT() FUNCTION CALL CONDITIONS**’ section. ![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/lux-algo/alerts/conditions.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=8595c79976bfc499cf7b931eae6ca39a) Toggle on the conditions of interest. Now create a new alert, in the first **Condition** drop-down menu select the **LuxAlgo Premium** indicator, in the second drop-down menu select **Any alert() function call**, you can then create the alert.

This alert would use **once per bar close** by default.

![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/lux-algo/alerts/image117.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=73c7a5fc79ce19b4c95a7655d48be2c8)

All-in-one alerts do not differ from regular alerts, they will be using the same indicator settings as the one used during their creation. Note however that you cannot set a custom message for all-in-one alerts, the message displayed when the selected conditions trigger will be the same as the one used in the same individual alert conditions.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/alerts#any-alert-function-call-message)

Any Alert() Function Call Message

Users can set a custom message that will be used when an “any alert() function call” condition is triggered in the message field below the list of conditions. Users can use placeholders to customize messages and return useful information, the following placeholders are supported:

#### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/alerts#symbol-placeholders)

Symbol Placeholders

| Placeholder | Description | Example |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `{default}` | Default message associated with the triggered condition | `"Bullish Confirmation Signal"` |
| `{ticker}` | Symbol ticker without the exchange prefix | `"MSFT"` |
| `{exchange}` | Symbol exchange/data source | `"COINBASE"` |
| `{sector}` | Sector of the symbol, `na` if the symbol has no sector | `"Technology Services"` |
| `{market}` | Symbol market type | `"Stocks"` |

#### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/alerts#time-placeholders)

Time Placeholders

| Placeholder | Description | Example |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `{tf}` | Chart timeframe, includes “S” for seconds, “D” for days, “W” for weeks, “M” for months | `"15"` |
| `{time}` | Unix time in milliseconds in exchange timezone | `"1705331385158"` |
| `{year}` | Current year in exchange timezone | `"2024"` |
| `{month}` | Current month in exchange timezone | `"7"` |
| `{day}` | Current day of the month in exchange timezone | `"21"` |

#### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/alerts#data-placeholders)

Data Placeholders

| Placeholder | Description | Example |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `{open}` | Opening price | `"1.2145"` |
| `{high}` | High price | `"1.2357"` |
| `{low}` | Low price | `"1.1983"` |
| `{close}` | Closing price | `"1.0569"` |
| `{volume}` | Current volume | `"45216"` |

#### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/alerts#indicators-placeholders)

Indicators Placeholders

| Placeholder | Description | Example |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `{smart_trail}` | Smart Trail overlay value | `"0.8321"` |
| `{rz_r3}` | Reversal Zones overlay resistance 3 value | `"3.4102"` |
| `{rz_r2}` | Reversal Zones overlay resistance 2 value | `"1.0293"` |
| `{rz_r1}` | Reversal Zones overlay resistance 1 value | `"5.1234"` |
| `{rz_s1}` | Reversal Zones overlay support 1 value | `"2.5647"` |
| `{rz_s2}` | Reversal Zones overlay support 2 value | `"7.8910"` |
| `{rz_s3}` | Reversal Zones overlay support 3 value | `"6.2345"` |
| `{catcher}` | Trend Catcher overlay value | `"4.3456"` |
| `{tracer}` | Trend Tracer overlay value | `"3.7812"` |
| `{neo_lead}` | Neo Cloud overlay lead value | `"1.9087"` |
| `{neo_lag}` | Neo Cloud overlay lag value | `"0.4571"` |
| `{tp1}` | Take Profit 1 value | `"2.7690"` |
| `{sl1}` | Stop Loss 1 value | `"8.1203"` |
| `{tp2}` | Take Profit 2 value | `"9.6584"` |
| `{sl2}` | Stop Loss 2 | `"3.1246"` |

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/alerts#format-as-json)

Format as JSON

Use the following message template to receive “any alert() function call” messages in the JSON format:

    {
      "alert": "{default}",
      "ticker": "{ticker}",
      "tf": "{tf}",
      "ohlcv":{
        "open": {open},
        "high": {high},
        "low": {low},
        "close": {close},
        "volume": {volume}
      },
      "bartime": {time}
    }
    

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/alerts#updating-alerts-using-any-alert-function-call)

Updating Alerts Using Any Alert() Function Call

If you already set an _any alert() function call_ alert and want to change the indicator settings or want to toggle on another condition all you need to do is edit the alert you want to update, select the second instance of the indicator in the first **Condition** drop-down menu and then click on save. ![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/lux-algo/alerts/image345.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=c7cf55887713e989406137742e57cf8f)

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/alerts#custom-alert-creator)

Custom Alert Creator
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/lux-algo/alerts/custom.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=5b994868be8eb9b4e050a54b0143f5e6) Users wishing to construct more complex alerts using features within the toolkit and/or external indicators can use the **Custom Alert Creator**. The custom alert creator allows alerting when various user-set conditions are met or when a sequence of conditions is complete.

A user wishing to be alerted when any bullish signal occurs while the smart trail is bullish could do it as follows:![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/lux-algo/alerts/custom_example.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=dc47b4f30d1f6051ce03760adad7f99e)

A custom alert can be triggered as an _any alert() function call_ if the setting is selected or as a regular alert when selected in the Tradingview alert creator menu.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/alerts#steps)

Steps

Steps allow creating a sequence of conditions, which when met trigger an alert. When a condition with a step equal to 1 is met the next condition associated with step 2 will be evaluated (if enabled) and so on for higher steps (if any). Conditions with the same associated step will require both conditions to be true in order for the condition associated with a higher step (if any) to be evaluated. This allows certain conditions to act as filters.

A user wishing to be alerted for any bullish confirmation signal classified as 1 or 2 by the ML Classifier occurring after the smart trail turned bullish could do it as follows:![](https://mintcdn.com/luxalgo/-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4/public/images/lux-algo/alerts/step_example.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=-Cu8R2acNraf_ZS4&q=85&s=b727690a7bb16e1ec2df294f17281561)_Make sure the ML Classifier is enabled_.

Make sure steps are set such that they form a linear sequence. For example, if the lowest step is 2 or if the set steps are only 1 and 3 an error will be returned.

#### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/alerts#or-step-operator)

OR Step Operator

The “OR” step operator can be used to get alerted for any additional condition using “OR” as step, in addition to other set custom alert conditions. Conditions using the “OR” step can be highlighted using a different color, which can be set from the Custom Alert Creator settings. Users can choose the location of this visual element (top or bottom of the chart).

#### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/alerts#all-step-operator)

All Step Operator

The “All” step operator can be used to filter any set “Step” condition, including “OR” and “Invalidate”. This step operator can be useful if all the steps in a sequence needs to obey a specific rule.

If a user has 2 steps set, and requires both of these to occur at a specific time interval such as 9am to 1pm, then we can use a “Session” condition using the “All” step, requiring our step 1 and step 2 to be occur between 9am and 1pm.

#### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/alerts#invalidate-step)

Invalidate Step

The “Invalidate” step allows to set a condition as an “invalidation condition”. When this condition is triggered while a sequence of conditions is incomplete, the sequence will restart at step 1. If multiple steps are set as “Invalidate” any of the conditions being true will reset the sequence of conditions, as such not all of them are required to be true for the sequence of conditions to reset.

Example
-------

Let’s take an example where we use 2 regular steps and one “Invalidate” step. The alert will trigger when step 2 trigger after step 1 has been triggered.

1

[](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/alerts#)

Step 1

Step 1 condition trigger, we will now evaluate step 2 from now on.

2

[](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/alerts#)

Invalidation Step

Invalidation step condition trigger, we reset the sequence and evaluate step 1 just after.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/alerts#invalidation-behaviors)

Invalidation Behaviors

Invalidation behaviors allows adding more restrictions to a sequence of conditions, users can use two different invalidation behaviors described below:

#### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/alerts#invalidate-on-step-1)

Invalidate On Step 1

The “Invalidate On Step 1” behavior allows to reset an incomplete sequence of conditions when the condition on step 1 trigger. This prevents the first step condition from happening in between other steps of the condition sequence. This behavior is useful when the first step of our sequence of conditions needs to never be repeated during the sequence.

Example
-------

Let’s take an example where we use 3 regular steps.

1

[](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/alerts#)

Step 1

Step 1 condition trigger, we will now evaluate step 2 from now on.

2

[](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/alerts#)

Step 2

Step 2 condition trigger, we will now evaluate step 3 from now on.

3

[](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/alerts#)

Step 1 Trigger

Step 1 condition trigger, we start evaluating step 2 from now.

#### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/alerts#invalidate-on-any-repeated-step)

Invalidate On Any Repeated Step

The “Invalidate On Any Repeated Step” behavior allows to reset an incomplete sequence of conditions when a step is triggered such that it does not respect the set order of conditions. This behavior is useful when we want a perfectly ordered sequence of conditions to complete, without any step repeating itself.

Example
-------

Let’s take an example where we use 3 regular steps.

1

[](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/alerts#)

Step 1

Step 1 condition trigger, we will now evaluate step 2 from now on.

2

[](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/alerts#)

Step 2

Step 2 condition trigger, we will now evaluate step 3 from now on.

3

[](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/alerts#)

Step 1 or 2 Trigger

Step 1 or 2 conditions trigger, we start evaluating step 1 from now.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/alerts#maximum-step-interval)

Maximum Step Interval

Users can determine what is the maximum allowed horizontal distance (in bars) between two steps by enabling the “Maximum Step Interval” setting. This allows restricting steps separated by a large amount of bars. If the amount of bars since a step exceed the set threshold, then the conditions sequence is reset, and we start evaluating from step 1 again.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/alerts#highlight-on-chart)

Highlight On Chart

When a custom alert condition is set, a visual element is displayed at the bottom of the chart in order to more easily visualize when the custom alert conditions occurs (displayed by default).

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/alerts#alerts-reference)

Alerts Reference
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/alerts#pre-set-alerts)

Pre-Set Alerts

| Alert | Description |
| --- | --- |
| Any alert() function call | Return when an alert when a user toggled any alert() condition is triggered (see sections below) |
| Any Confirmation | Triggers when any Confirmation signal (bullish/bearish normal/+) is displayed |
| Any Bullish Confirmation | Triggers when any bullish Confirmation signal (normal/+) is displayed |
| Any Bearish Confirmation | Triggers when any bearish Confirmation signal (normal/+) is displayed |
| Any Confirmation+ | Triggers when any Confirmation + signal (bullish/bearish) is displayed |
| Any Contrarian | Triggers when any Contrarian signal (normal/+ bullish/bearish) is displayed |
| Any Bullish Contrarian | Triggers when any bullish Contrarian signal (normal/+) is displayed |
| Any Bearish Contrarian | Triggers when any bearish Contrarian signal (normal/+) is displayed |
| Bullish Confirmation | Triggers when a normal bullish Confirmation signal is displayed |
| Bearish Confirmation | Triggers when a normal bearish Confirmation signal is displayed |
| Bullish Confirmation+ | Triggers when a bullish Confirmation+ signal is displayed |
| Bearish Confirmation+ | Triggers when a bearish Confirmation+ signal is displayed |
| Bullish Exit | Triggers when a bullish exit signal is displayed |
| Bearish Exit | Triggers when a bearish exit signal is displayed |
| Trend Catcher Down | Triggers once the Trend Catcher starts decreasing (switch from green to red) |
| Trend Catcher Up | Triggers once the Trend Catcher starts rising (switch from red to green) |
| Trend Tracer Down | Triggers once the Trend Tracer starts decreasing (switch from green to red) |
| Trend Tracer Up | Triggers once the Trend Tracer starts rising (switch from red to green) |
| Custom Alert Condition | Triggers on the event of a user set custom alert condition being true |

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/alerts#any-alert-function-call-2)

Any alert() Function Call

| Alert | Description | Default |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Bullish Confirmation | Triggers when a normal bullish Confirmation signal is displayed |     |
| Bearish Confirmation | Triggers when a normal bearish Confirmation signal is displayed |     |
| Bullish + | Triggers when a strong bullish Confirmation signal is displayed |     |
| Bearish + | Triggers when a strong bearish Confirmation signal is displayed |     |
| Bullish Contrarian | Triggers when a normal bullish Contrarian signal is displayed |     |
| Bearish Contrarian | Triggers when a normal bearish Contrarian signal is displayed |     |
| Bullish + | Triggers when a strong bullish Contrarian signal is displayed |     |
| Bearish + | Triggers when a strong bearish Contrarian signal is displayed |     |
| Bullish Exit | Triggers when a bullish exit signal is displayed |     |
| Bearish Exit | Triggers when a bearish exit signal is displayed |     |
| Take Profit | Triggers when a take profit is reached (TP1 or TP2) |     |
| Stop Loss | Triggers when a stop loss is reached (SL1 or SL2) |     |
| Bullish Turn + | Triggers when a weak bullish trend turns strong (purple candle switch to green) |     |
| Bearish Turn + | Triggers when a weak bearish trend turns strong (purple candle switch to red) |     |
| Custom Alert Condition | Triggers on the event of a user set custom alert condition being true |     |

To open the settings menu, place your mouse pointer over the indicator title on your chart, you will then see a list of icons appear, and click on the gear ⚙️ icon.You can also open the settings panel by double-clicking any element displayed by the toolkit.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#smart-money-flow)

Smart Money Flow
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#show-money-flow)

Show Money Flow

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-toggle)

Toggle

default: true

Display Smart Money Flow oscillator

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#money-flow)

Money Flow

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-numerical-input)

Numerical Input

default: 35

Money flow oscillator length, higher values will highlight longer term money flow.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#smooth)

Smooth

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-numerical-input-1)

Numerical Input

default: 6

Money flow oscillator smoothing amount, higher values will return a smoother Money Flow oscillator.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#hyerwave)

HyerWave
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#show-hyerwave)

Show HyerWave

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-toggle-1)

Toggle

default: true

Display HyperWave oscillator

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#hyperwave-length)

HyperWave Length

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-numerical-input-2)

Numerical Input

default: 7

HyperWave length setting. Higher values will highlight longer term variations from the HyperWave oscillator.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#signal)

Signal

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-dropdown)

Dropdown

String

Show Expand

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-sma)

SMA

default:true

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-trailing-stop)

Trailing Stop

Type of signal line displayed alongside the HyperWave.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-numerical-input-3)

Numerical Input

default: 3

Length of the signal method applied to the HyperWave oscillator, higher values will return longer term signals returned from the HyperWave.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#colors)

Colors

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-numerical-input-4)

Numerical Input

default: 80

Transparency of the area between the HyperWave and its signal plot.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#hyperwave-divergences)

HyperWave Divergences
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#divergences-sensitivity-%)

Divergences Sensitivity %

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-numerical-input-5)

Numerical Input

default: 10

Sensitivity of the divergences detection algorithm, with lower values will return fewer and longer-term divergences.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#show-divergences)

Show Divergences

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-toggle-2)

Toggle

default: true

Display divergences between the price and HyperWave oscillator on the oscillator pane.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#show-divergences-on-chart)

Show Divergences On Chart

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-toggle-3)

Toggle

default: true

Display divergences between the price and HyperWave oscillator on the price chart.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#reversals)

Reversals
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#reversal-factor)

Reversal Factor

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-dropdown-1)

Dropdown

Numerical

Show Expand

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-1)

1

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-2)

2

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-3)

3

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-4)

4

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-5)

5

default:true

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-6)

6

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-7)

7

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-8)

8

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-9)

9

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-10)

10

Controls the frequency at which reversals are detected by the HyperWave, with higher values returning less frequent and longer term potential reversals.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#show-reversals)

Show Reversals

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-toggle-4)

Toggle

default: true

Display reversal signals at the top/bottom of the indicator pane.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#confluence)

Toggle

default: false

Display confluence meter.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#meter-width)

Meter Width

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-numerical)

Numerical

default: 3

Width of the confluence meter.

Custom Alert Creator
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#money-flow-2)

Money Flow

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-toggle-8)

Toggle

default: false

Enable the selected Money Flow condition to be used in the custom alert creator.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-dropdown-2)

Dropdown

String

Show Expand

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-greater-than)

Greater Than

default:true

Lower Than

Crossing Over

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-crossing-under)

Crossing Under

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-crossing)

Crossing

Comparison operator used to compare the current Money Flow value with the inline numerical input.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-numerical-input-6)

Numerical Input

default: 50

Value used to compare the Money Flow with.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#invalidation-behavior)

Invalidation Behavior

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-dropdown-27)

Dropdown

Numerical

Show Expand

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-none)

None

default:true

No invalidation behavior.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-invalidate-on-step-1)

Invalidate On Step 1

The “Invalidate On Step 1” behavior allows to reset an incomplete sequence of conditions when the condition on step 1 trigger. This prevents the first step condition from happening in between other steps of the condition sequence.This behavior is useful when the first step of our sequence of conditions needs to never be repeated during the sequence.

Example
-------

Let’s take an example where we use 3 regular steps.

1

[](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#)

Step 1

Step 1 condition trigger, we will now evaluate step 2 from now on.

2

[](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#)

Step 2

Step 2 condition trigger, we will now evaluate step 3 from now on.

3

[](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#)

Step 1 Trigger

Step 1 condition trigger, we start evaluating step 2 from now.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-invalidate-on-any-repeated-step)

Invalidate On Any Repeated Step

The “Invalidate On Any Repeated Step” behavior allows to reset an incomplete sequence of conditions when a step is triggered such that it does not respect the user-set order of conditions.This behavior is useful when we want a perfectly ordered sequence of conditions to complete, without any step repeating itself.

Example
-------

Let’s take an example where we use 3 regular steps.

1

[](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#)

Step 1

Step 1 condition trigger, we will now evaluate step 2 from now on.

2

[](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#)

Step 2

Step 2 condition trigger, we will now evaluate step 3 from now on.

3

[](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#)

Step 1 or 2 Trigger

Step 1 or 2 conditions trigger, we start evaluating step 1 from now.

Invalidation behaviors allows adding more restrictions to a sequence of conditions, users can use two different invalidation behaviors described below.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#maximum-step-interval)

Maximum Step Interval

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-numerical-input-11)

Numerical Input

default:10

Maximum allowed horizontal distance (in bars) between two steps. If the amount of bars since a step exceed the selected threshold, then the conditions sequence is reset, and we start evaluating from step 1 again.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#highlight-custom-alert-triggers)

Highlight Custom Alert Triggers

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-toggle-18)

Toggle

default:true

When a custom alert condition is set, a visual element is displayed at the bottom of the chart in order to more easily visualize when the custom alert conditions occurs (displayed by default).

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#calculation)

Calculation
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#calculated-bars)

Calculated Bars

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/oscillator-matrix/settings#param-numerical-1)

Numerical

default:10000

Amount of most recent bars used for the calculation of the toolkit. Lower values allow returning faster computation times.

Was this page helpful?

YesNo

To open the settings menu, place your mouse pointer over the indicator title on your chart, you will then see a list of icons appear, and click on the gear ⚙️ icon.You can also open the settings panel by double-clicking any element displayed by the toolkit.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#basic-settings)

Basic Settings
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#presets-/-filters)

Presets / Filters

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-dropdown)

Dropdown

String

Show Expand

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-none)

None

none

default:true

No presets/filter enabled.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-trend-trader)

Trend Trader

preset

*   Confirmation Signals
*   Smart Trail
*   Trend Catcher

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-scalper)

Scalper

preset

*   Confirmation Signals
*   Confirmation gradient coloring
*   Reversal Zones
*   Take Profit/Stop Losses

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-swing-trader)

Swing Trader

preset

*   Confirmation Signals
*   Long-Term Frequency Autopilot
*   Simple confirmation candle coloring
*   Neo Cloud

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-contrarian-trader)

Contrarian Trader

preset

*   Contrarian Signals
*   Mid-Term Frequency Autopilot
*   Contrarian candle coloring
*   Reversal Zones

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-smart-trail)

Smart Trail

filter

Show bullish signals when price is above the Smart Trail, and bearish signals when price is under the Smart Trail.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-trend-tracer)

Trend Tracer

filter

Show bullish signals when Trend Tracer is indicating an up-trend, and bearish signals when Trend Tracer is indicating a down-trend.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-trend-catcher)

Trend Catcher

filter

Show bullish signals when Trend Catcher is indicating an up-trend, and bearish signals when Trend Catcher is indicating a down-trend.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-neo-cloud)

Neo Cloud

filter

Show bullish signals above Neo cloud, and bearish signals under Neo Cloud.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-trend-strength)

Trend Strength

filter

Show bullish/bearish signals when the Trend strength is above 50%.

Presets allows users to easily enable multiple features at once from a selected option.

Note that when a preset is selected some settings such as the toggles of the displayed overlay indicators can become inactive/not usable. If you wish to further customize the Signals & Overlays® toolkit, we suggest disabling the Preset and manually customizing the settings.

On the other hand, filters allow users to display confirmation/contrarian signals when a specific overlay or metric behavior is respected.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#signal-mode)

Signal Mode

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-dropdown-1)

Dropdown

String

Show Expand

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-confirmation-exits)

Confirmation + Exits

default:true

Confirmation signals alongside exit signals.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-contrarian-exits)

Contrarian + Exits

Contrarian signals alongside exit signals.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-none-1)

None

No signals.

Controls the type of signal generation algorithm to use.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#ml-signal-classifier)

ML Signal Classifier

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-toggle)

Toggle

default: false

Enable the ML Classifier for the returned signals. Signals will be classified between groups 1, 2, 3, and 4, with 1/2 indicating replacements and 3/4 signals in accordance with a main trend.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#signals-sensitivity)

Signals Sensitivity

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-numerical-input)

Numerical Input

default: 12

The sensitivity setting controls how sensitive the signals generation algorithms are to shorter term price variations, with higher values of the setting returning longer term signals. To learn more about signal settings see the following [page](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings)
.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#candle-coloring)

Candle Coloring

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-dropdown-2)

Dropdown

String

Show Expand

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-confirmation-simple)

Confirmation Simple

default:true

Color candles using three shades based on the Confirmation signal algorithm.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-confirmation-gradient)

Confirmation Gradient

Color candles using a gradient based on the Confirmation signal algorithm.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-contrarian-gradient)

Contrarian Gradient

Color candles using a gradient based on the Contrarian signal algorithm.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-none-2)

None

Change the color of the candle/bars on the user chart based on the selected option. To learn more about candle coloring see the following [page](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/candle-coloring)
.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#indicator-overlay)

Take Profits/Stop Losses
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#tp/sl-levels)

TP/SL Levels

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-dropdown-8)

Dropdown

String

Show Expand

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-none-3)

None

default:true

No take profits/stop losses levels are displayed.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-signals)

Signals

default:true

Return take profits/stop losses levels based on Confirmation/Contrarian signals.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-smart-trail-1)

Smart Trail

default:true

Return take profits/stop losses levels based on Smart Trail sentiment changes.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-reversal-zones)

Reversal Zones

default:true

Return take profits/stop losses levels based on the contact between the price and Reversal Zones extremities.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-trend-catcher-1)

Trend Catcher

default:true

Return take profits/stop losses levels based on the Trend Catcher sentiment changes.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-trend-tracer-1)

Trend Tracer

default:true

Return take profits/stop losses levels based on the Trend Tracer sentiment changes.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-neo-cloud-1)

Neo Cloud

default:true

Return take profits/stop losses levels based on the Neo Cloud sentiment changes.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-custom-alert-creator)

Custom Alert Creator

default:true

Return take profits/stop losses levels based on the user set custom alert creator condition triggering. Unlike other options this one assumes a bullish sentiment, returning take profits above the price and stop losses below the price.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#distance)

Distance

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-numerical-input-1)

Numerical Input

default: 5

Control how far away take profits/stop losses levels are located from the price, with higher values returning levels located farther away from the price.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#advanced-settings)

Advanced Settings
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#ml-classifier)

ML Classifier

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-numerical-input-2)

Numerical Input

default: 1234

ML Classifier filter. This input allows filtering out classified signals that are not specified in the input. For example if the input only contains `12` then only signals classified as either 1 or 2 will be displayed.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#autopilot-sensitivity)

Autopilot Sensitivity

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-dropdown-9)

Dropdown

String

Show Expand

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-off)

Off

default:true

Disable the autopilot sensitivity algorithm.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-short-term)

Short-Term

Enable the autopilot sensitivity algorithm to return shorter term signals.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-medium-term)

Medium-Term

Enable the autopilot sensitivity algorithm to return medium term signals.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-long-term)

Long-Term

Enable the autopilot sensitivity algorithm to return longer term signals.

Allows enabling autopilot sensitivity for the selected signal algorithm. When autopilot is enabled changes in the `sensitivity` settings will not affect signals.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#dashboard)

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#invalidation-behavior)

Invalidation Behavior

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-dropdown-38)

Dropdown

Numerical

Show Expand

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-none-4)

None

default:true

No invalidation behavior.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-invalidate-on-step-1)

Invalidate On Step 1

The “Invalidate On Step 1” behavior allows to reset an incomplete sequence of conditions when the condition on step 1 trigger. This prevents the first step condition from happening in between other steps of the condition sequence.This behavior is useful when the first step of our sequence of conditions needs to never be repeated during the sequence.

Example
-------

Let’s take an example where we use 3 regular steps.

1

[](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#)

Step 1

Step 1 condition trigger, we will now evaluate step 2 from now on.

2

[](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#)

Step 2

Step 2 condition trigger, we will now evaluate step 3 from now on.

3

[](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#)

Step 1 Trigger

Step 1 condition trigger, we start evaluating step 2 from now.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-invalidate-on-any-repeated-step)

Invalidate On Any Repeated Step

The “Invalidate On Any Repeated Step” behavior allows to reset an incomplete sequence of conditions when a step is triggered such that it does not respect the user-set order of conditions.This behavior is useful when we want a perfectly ordered sequence of conditions to complete, without any step repeating itself.

Example
-------

Let’s take an example where we use 3 regular steps.

1

[](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#)

Step 1

Step 1 condition trigger, we will now evaluate step 2 from now on.

2

[](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#)

Step 2

Step 2 condition trigger, we will now evaluate step 3 from now on.

3

[](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#)

Step 1 or 2 Trigger

Step 1 or 2 conditions trigger, we start evaluating step 1 from now.

Invalidation behaviors allows adding more restrictions to a sequence of conditions, users can use two different invalidation behaviors described below.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#maximum-step-interval)

Maximum Step Interval

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-numerical-input-6)

Numerical Input

default:10

Maximum allowed horizontal distance (in bars) between two steps. If the amount of bars since a step exceed the selected threshold, then the conditions sequence is reset, and we start evaluating from step 1 again.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#highlight-custom-alert-triggers)

Highlight Custom Alert Triggers

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/signals-overlays/settings#param-toggle-21)

Toggle

default:true

When a custom alert condition is set, a visual element is displayed at the bottom of the chart in order to more easily visualize when the custom alert conditions occurs (displayed by default).

To open the settings menu, place your mouse pointer over the indicator title on your chart, you will then see a list of icons appear, and click on the gear ⚙️ icon.You can also open the settings panel by double-clicking any element displayed by the toolkit.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#market-structure)

Market Structure
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#internal)

Internal

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-dropdown)

Dropdown

String

Show Expand

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-all)

All

default:true

Show all types of internal market structures.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-c-ho-ch-all)

CHoCH (All)

Show all types of change of characters (CHoCH).

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-c-ho-ch)

CHoCH+

Only show “supported” change of characters (CHoCH+).

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-c-ho-ch)

CHoCH

Only show “leading” change of characters (CHoCH).

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-bos)

BOS

Only show break of structures (BOS).

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-none)

None

Show no internal market structure.

Type of internal market structures to display.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-numerical)

Numerical

default: 5

Determines the sensitivity of the swing detection algorithm.Higher values will return longer-term swing points, and as such longer-term internal market structures.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#swing)

Swing

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-dropdown-1)

Dropdown

String

Show Expand

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-all-1)

All

default:true

Show all types of swing market structures.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-c-ho-ch-all-1)

CHoCH (All)

Show all types of change of characters (CHoCH).

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-c-ho-ch-1)

CHoCH+

Only show “supported” change of characters (CHoCH+).

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-c-ho-ch-1)

CHoCH

Only show “leading” change of characters (CHoCH).

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-bos-1)

BOS

Only show break of structures (BOS).

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-none-1)

None

Show no swing market structure.

Type of swing market structures to display.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-numerical-1)

Numerical

default: 50

Determines the sensitivity of the swing detection algorithm.Higher values will return longer-term swing points, and as such longer-term swing market structures.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#timeframe)

Timeframe

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-timeframe)

Timeframe

default: Chart

Chart timeframe used for the detection of internal and swing market structures.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#show-swing-high/low)

Show Swing High/Low

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-toggle)

Toggle

default: false

Display detected swing points when enabled.

Detected swing points are displayed retrospectively, and as such do not appear in real-time.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#show-strong/weak-hl)

Show Strong/Weak HL

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-toggle-1)

Toggle

default: false

Display strong/weak swing levels when enabled.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#color-candles)

Color Candles

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-toggle-2)

Toggle

default: false

Color user chart candles based on the trend detected from internal market structures as follows:

*   Bullish CHoCH: Dark Green
*   Bullish BOS: Bright Green
*   Bearish BOS: Bright Red
*   Bearish CHoCH: Dark Red

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#volumetric-order-blocks)

Volumetric Order Blocks
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#show-last)

Show Last

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-toggle-3)

Toggle

default: true

Display volumetric order blocks.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-numerical-2)

Numerical

default: 5

Determines how many of the most recent volumetric order blocks to display on the chart.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#internal-buy/sell-activity)

Internal Buy/Sell Activity

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-toggle-4)

Toggle

default: true

Display volumetric order blocks.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#show-breakers)

Show Breakers

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-toggle-5)

Toggle

default: false

Display breaker blocks.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#length)

Length

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-numerical-3)

Numerical

default: 5

Determines the sensitivity of the swing detection algorithm used to detect order blocks.Higher values will return longer-term swing points, and as such longer-term order blocks.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#mitigation-method)

Mitigation Method

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-dropdown-2)

Dropdown

String

Show Expand

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-close)

Close

default:true

Mitigate order blocks using the closing price.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-wick)

Wick

Mitigate order blocks using candle wicks (high/low price).

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-average)

Average

Mitigate order blocks using the crossing from the closing price and the order block area average level.

Determines the method used to mitigate order blocks.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#timeframe-2)

Timeframe

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-timeframe-1)

Timeframe

default: Chart

Chart timeframe used for the detection of order blocks.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#show-metrics)

Show Metrics

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-toggle-6)

Toggle

default: true

Display order block metrics such as total volume and percentage located at the right of the chart.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#show-mid-line)

Show Mid-Line

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-toggle-7)

Toggle

default: true

Display order block area average level (dashed line).

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#hide-overlap)

Hide Overlap

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-toggle-8)

Toggle

default: true

Hide overlapping order blocks, conserving the most recent one.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#liquidity-concepts)

Toggle

default: false

Dropdown

Numerical

Show Expand

1

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-2)

2

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-3)

3

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-4)

4

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-5)

5

default:true

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-6)

6

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-7)

7

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-8)

8

9

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-10)

10

Determines the sensitivity of the swing detection algorithm used to detect patterns. Higher values will return longer-term swing points, and as such longer-term patterns.

###

Show Patterns Zones

Toggle

default: true

Display zones around the pattern lines.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#equal-h&l)

Equal H&L

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-toggle-12)

Toggle

default: false

Display equal highs/lows on the chart.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-dropdown-4)

Dropdown

String

Show Expand

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-short-term)

Short-Term

default:true

Use short term swing point detection for detecting equal highs/lows, returning shorter term EQHL as a result.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-long-term)

Long-Term

Use long term swing point detection for detecting equal highs/lows, returning longer term EQHL as a result.

Determines the sensitivity of the swing detection algorithm used to detect equal highs/lows.

Toggle

default: false

Display liquidity grabs on the chart.

Imbalance Concepts
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

* * *

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-toggle-14)

Toggle

default: false

Display the selected imbalance on the chart.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-dropdown-5)

Dropdown

String

Show Expand

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-fvg)

FVG

default:true

Detect fair value gaps (FVG) when selected.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-inverse-fvg)

Inverse FVG

Detect inverse fair value gaps when selected.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-double-fvg)

Double FVG

Detect double fair value gaps when selected.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-volume-imbalance)

Volume Imbalance

Detect volume imbalances when selected.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-opening-gap)

Opening Gap

default:true

Detect opening gaps when selected.

Determines which imbalance to detect.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#mitigation-method-2)

Mitigation Method

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-dropdown-6)

Dropdown

String

Show Expand

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-close-1)

Close

default:true

Mitigate imbalances using the closing price.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-wick-1)

Wick

Mitigate imbalancess using candle wicks (high/low price).

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-average-1)

Average

Mitigate imbalances using the crossing from the closing price and the imbalance area average level.

Determines the method used to mitigate imbalances.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#timeframe-3)

Timeframe

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-timeframe-2)

Timeframe

default: Chart

Chart timeframe used for the detection of imbalances.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#extend-imbalance)

Extend Imbalance

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-numerical-5)

Numerical

default: 10

Extend the imbalance area to the right by the selected amount of bars.

### 

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#volatility-threshold)

Volatility Threshold

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-numerical-6)

Numerical

default: 0

Threshold used to filter out imbalances with a low area height. Higher values will preserver more volatility imbalances.

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#anchor-to-origin)

Anchor To Origin

[​](https://docs.luxalgo.com/docs/algos/price-action-concepts/settings#param-toggle-22)

Toggle

default: true

Set the left anchor of the retracement to the appropriate coordinate depending on the selected extremities. Else the most recent bar will be used as anchor.
